====New Popular Front====
[[File:Répartition des circonscriptions du Nouveau Front populaire (NFP).svg|thumb|upright=2|Map of constituencies by the primary party affiliation of [[New Popular Front]] candidates]]
[[File:Affiche Nouveau Front populaire Votez.jpg|thumb|left|upright|New Popular Front campaign poster]]
Leftist politician [[François Ruffin]] called on all left-wing parties, including [[The Ecologists (France)|The Ecologists]] (LE), to form a "[[popular front]]" in order to avoid the "worst" outcome.<ref>{{Cite web|date=9 June 2024|title=Macron dissolves the French parliament and calls a snap election after defeat in EU vote|url=https://apnews.com/article/france-european-election-national-rally-marine-lepen-b132616d24de829660d8dbe0659e50fd|access-date=10 June 2024|website=Associated Press|language=en|archive-date=28 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240628211113/https://apnews.com/article/france-european-election-national-rally-marine-lepen-b132616d24de829660d8dbe0659e50fd|url-status=live}}</ref> Calls for unity were also shared by [[Socialist Party (France)|Socialist Party]] (PS) leader [[Olivier Faure]], LE leader [[Marine Tondelier]] and [[French Communist Party]] (PCF) leader [[Fabien Roussel]].<ref>{{Cite web|date=10 June 2024|title='Win together or lose separately?': French left calls for unity ahead of snap elections|url=https://www.france24.com/en/europe/20240610-france-french-left-calls-unity-ahead-snap-legislative-elections-nupes-melenchon-far-right|access-date=11 June 2024|website=France 24|language=en|archive-date=10 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240610221008/https://www.france24.com/en/europe/20240610-france-french-left-calls-unity-ahead-snap-legislative-elections-nupes-melenchon-far-right|url-status=live}}</ref> A letter of 350 intellectuals (including [[Esther Duflo]] and [[Annie Ernaux]]) calling for a union of left-wing forces was published in ''[[Le Monde]]'' on 10 June.<ref>{{Cite news|date=10 June 2024|title=" L'union des gauches et des écologistes, maintenant ! " : l'appel de 350 personnalités du monde politique, intellectuel, militant et artistique|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/idees/article/2024/06/10/l-union-des-gauches-et-des-ecologistes-maintenant-l-appel-de-350-personnalites-du-monde-politique-intellectuel-militant-et-artistique_6238475_3232.html|access-date=|work=Le Monde|language=fr|archive-date=14 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240614110840/https://www.lemonde.fr/idees/article/2024/06/10/l-union-des-gauches-et-des-ecologistes-maintenant-l-appel-de-350-personnalites-du-monde-politique-intellectuel-militant-et-artistique_6238475_3232.html|url-status=live}}</ref> The [[New Popular Front]] was established on the same day, bringing together [[La France Insoumise]] (LFI), the PS, LE, the PCF, [[Place Publique]], and various other political forces.<ref name="Garnier">{{Cite news|last=Garnier|first=Hugues|date=10 June 2024|title=Programme, candidature unique... Les partis de gauche appellent à créer un "nouveau Front populaire"|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/europeennes/programme-candidature-unique-les-partis-de-gauche-appellent-a-creer-un-nouveau-front-populaire_AN-202406100931.html|access-date=12 June 2024|website=BFMTV|language=fr|archive-date=11 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240611100209/https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/europeennes/programme-candidature-unique-les-partis-de-gauche-appellent-a-creer-un-nouveau-front-populaire_AN-202406100931.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

On 13 June, LFI, the PS, LE, and the PCF reached an agreement on how to allocate 546 constituencies (including metropolitan France and French voters living abroad) between candidates of their choice, obtaining 229, 175, 92, and 50 constituencies, respectively, with these seats divided among themselves and allied forces.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Nutarelli|first1=Mathilde|title=Nouveau Front populaire : la répartition des circonscriptions est bouclée, les partis désignent leurs candidats|url=https://www.publicsenat.fr/actualites/politique/nouveau-front-populaire-la-repartition-des-circonscriptions-est-bouclee-les-partis-designent-leurs-candidats|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Public Sénat|date=14 June 2024|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630225609/https://www.publicsenat.fr/actualites/politique/nouveau-front-populaire-la-repartition-des-circonscriptions-est-bouclee-les-partis-designent-leurs-candidats|url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|last1=Paillassa|first1=Pauline|title=Elections législatives 2024 : visualisez la répartition des circonscriptions entre les partis du Nouveau Front populaire|url=https://www.francetvinfo.fr/elections/legislatives/infographies-elections-legislatives-2024-visualisez-la-repartition-des-circonscriptions-entre-les-partis-du-nouveau-front-populaire_6604014.html|access-date=22 June 2024|work=franceinfo|date=14 June 2024|archive-date=21 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240621114306/https://www.francetvinfo.fr/elections/legislatives/infographies-elections-legislatives-2024-visualisez-la-repartition-des-circonscriptions-entre-les-partis-du-nouveau-front-populaire_6604014.html|url-status=live}}</ref> After outcry from other members of the alliance, [[Adrien Quatennens]], previously convicted of domestic violence, withdrew his candidacy in [[Nord's 1st constituency]] on 16 June.<ref>{{cite news|title=Adrien Quatennens, investi par LFI, renonce à se présenter dans le Nord pour les élections législatives|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/16/adrien-quatennens-investi-par-lfi-renonce-a-se-presenter-dans-le-nord-pour-les-elections-legislatives_6240782_823448.html|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Le Monde|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=16 June 2024|archive-date=19 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240619095213/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/16/adrien-quatennens-investi-par-lfi-renonce-a-se-presenter-dans-le-nord-pour-les-elections-legislatives_6240782_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref> Several incumbent LFI deputies critical of leader Mélenchon – [[Alexis Corbière]], [[Raquel Garrido]], [[Hendrik Davi]], and [[Danielle Simonnet]] – were not renominated in their constituencies under the banner of the New Popular Front, a decision critiqued both by their supporters and other party leaders within the alliance. Nevertheless, the four candidates maintained their candidacies against LFI opponents in their constituencies. [[Frédéric Mathieu]], another Mélenchon critic within LFI, was also not renominated and opted not to run for re-election.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Cassini|first1=Sandrine|title=La France insoumise continue de compliquer la tâche du Nouveau Front populaire|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/17/la-france-insoumise-continue-de-compliquer-la-tache-du-nouveau-front-populaire_6240870_823448.html|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Le Monde|date=17 June 2024|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630225609/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/17/la-france-insoumise-continue-de-compliquer-la-tache-du-nouveau-front-populaire_6240870_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

The coalition unveiled its campaign platform on 14 June, which included overturning Macron's [[2023 French pension reform law|pension]], unemployment, education, immigration, police, [[Revenu de solidarité active|guaranteed minimum income]], and [[service national universel|universal national service]] reforms, as well as his cuts to funding for [[HLM|low-income housing]] and his merger of French nuclear safety organisations; lowering the retirement age to 60 in the longer-term; implementing price freezes on essential food, energy, and gas; raising the [[minimum wage]] to €1,600 per month (representing a 14% increase) and personalised housing assistance by 10%; moving towards a 32-hour work week for arduous or night shift jobs; conditioning government support for businesses on adherence to environmental, social, and anti-discriminatory regulations; reserving workers one-third of seats on boards of directors; increasing [[financial transaction tax]]es; banning bank financing for fossil fuels; nationalising control over water; reforming the [[Generalized Social Contribution|generalised social contribution]] and inheritance taxes (capping the latter), as well as nearly tripling the number of income tax brackets from 5 to 14, to make them more progressive; re-instituting a [[solidarity tax on wealth]] "with a climate component"; enacting an exit tax on funds withdrawn from the country; charging a [[vehicle miles traveled tax]] on imports; guaranteeing a price floor for agricultural products; cancelling the [[Comprehensive Economic and Trade Agreement]] and any future free trade treaties; and forbidding the imports of agricultural products which do not meet domestic social and environmental standards.<ref name="LMNFP"/>

Other key NFP proposals included raising the image and salaries of public healthcare, education, justice, and government jobs; strengthening the industrial sector in key strategic areas; establishing the right to [[menstrual leave]]; prohibiting new major highway projects; outlawing [[intensive animal farming]] and the usage of all [[Per- and polyfluoroalkyl substances|PFAS]]s, [[neonicotinoid]]s, and [[Glyphosate-based herbicides|glyphosate]]; re-examining the [[Common Agricultural Policy]]; providing partial or full government financing for home insulation; creating free public water fountains, showers, and toilets; constructing 200,000 new public housing units per year; requiring mandatory rent control in high-rent areas; introducing [[proportional representation]]; removing [[Article 49 of the French Constitution#Commitment of responsibility on a bill (49.3)|article 49.3]] from the constitution; outlawing the usage of [[blast ball]]s by riot police; continuing to supply weapons to defend Ukraine; [[International recognition of the State of Palestine|recognising]] the [[state of Palestine]] along with [[Israel]]; and demanding compliance with the [[International Court of Justice]] (ICJ) order against Israel and ceasing support for [[Benjamin Netanyahu]]'s government.<ref name="LMNFP">{{cite news|title=Ce que contient le programme du Nouveau Front populaire pour les élections législatives|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/14/ce-que-contient-le-programme-du-nouveau-front-populaire-pour-les-elections-legislatives_6239928_823448.html|access-date=26 June 2024|work=Le Monde|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=14 June 2024|archive-date=26 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240626010858/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/14/ce-que-contient-le-programme-du-nouveau-front-populaire-pour-les-elections-legislatives_6239928_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

[[File:Jean-Luc Mélenchon 2022 (cropped).jpg|thumb|upright|[[Jean-Luc Mélenchon]] in 2022]]

Opponents of the New Popular Front exploited uncertainty around who would be appointed prime minister in the event of the victory of the left, warning of the threat of [[Jean-Luc Mélenchon]]'s appointment given his refusal to recuse himself from the post; although on 22 June he said that he would be willing to be appointed prime minister, he claimed that he would "not impose" himself, even as numerous other potential appointees' names have circulated.<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives: Jean-Luc Mélenchon se dit "bien évidemment" prêt à devenir Premier ministre|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/legislatives-jean-luc-melenchon-se-dit-bien-evidemment-pret-a-devenir-premier-ministre_AD-202406220436.html|access-date=23 June 2024|work=BFMTV|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=22 June 2024|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630221003/https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/legislatives-jean-luc-melenchon-se-dit-bien-evidemment-pret-a-devenir-premier-ministre_AD-202406220436.html|url-status=live}}</ref> Other figures on the left, while reluctant to address the question of who they believed should be prime minister, were taken aback by his comments: former president [[François Hollande]], running in [[Corrèze's 1st constituency]], opined that Mélenchon should "keep his mouth shut," former prime minister [[Lionel Jospin]] said that he was hearing "just about everywhere, and particularly from voters of the left" that "Jean-Luc Mélenchon is not the solution," Fabien Roussel released a statement saying that "Mélenchon's nomination for the post of prime minister, [speculation about which] he himself is feeding into, has never been subject of an agreement between the forces of the Popular Front," Marine Tondelier, interviewed on LCI about Mélenchon's remarks, painted a generic portrait of the attributes of the ideal prime minister, ending with "and lastly, someone who unites."<ref>{{cite news|last1=Farge|first1=Baptiste|title=Hollande, Jospin, Roussel... L'hypothèse Mélenchon à Matignon crispe à gauche|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/la-france-insoumise/hollande-jospin-roussel-l-hypothese-melenchon-a-matignon-crispe-a-gauche_AV-202406240199.html|access-date=24 June 2024|work=BFMTV|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624152612/https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/la-france-insoumise/hollande-jospin-roussel-l-hypothese-melenchon-a-matignon-crispe-a-gauche_AV-202406240199.html|url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|title=EN DIRECT – Législatives : sur LCI, Gérald Darmanin veut "aider à reconstruire un projet" à droite|url=https://www.tf1info.fr/elections/en-direct-elections-legislatives-2024-campagne-rn-nfp-majorite-macron-bardella-attal-bompard-les-dernieres-informations-aujourd-hui-dimanche-23-juin-j-7-une-semaine-premier-tour-2305311.html|access-date=24 June 2024|work=LCI|date=23 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624020715/https://www.tf1info.fr/elections/en-direct-elections-legislatives-2024-campagne-rn-nfp-majorite-macron-bardella-attal-bompard-les-dernieres-informations-aujourd-hui-dimanche-23-juin-j-7-une-semaine-premier-tour-2305311.html|url-status=live}}</ref> In a pre-election Elabe poll, only 16% of respondents – including just 49% of Mélenchon's 2022 voters, 24% of supporters of green parties and 17% of Socialist Party supporters – indicated they would be supportive of his appointment as prime minister, compared to 83% against the idea.<ref>{{cite web|title=Les Français et les élections législatives|url=https://elabe.fr/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/12062024_elabe_bfmtv_les-francais-et-les-elections-legislatives.pdf|publisher=Elabe|access-date=24 June 2024|date=12 June 2024|archive-date=12 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240612162354/https://elabe.fr/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/12062024_elabe_bfmtv_les-francais-et-les-elections-legislatives.pdf|url-status=live}}</ref>

Infighting broke out into the open on 24 June, starting with PCF leader [[Fabien Roussel]]'s comments in the morning, "I say this to Jean-Luc Mélenchon: no one can proclaim himself Prime Minister," to which he added that the New Popular Front needed "the most unifying personality" to lead them in the incoming National Assembly which, according to him, would clearly not be Mélenchon,<ref>{{cite news|last1=Costentin|first1=Blandine|last2=Barbereau|first2=Stéphane|title=Législatives : "Jean-Luc Mélenchon n'est pas dans le paysage politique du Nouveau Front populaire" dit Fabien Roussel|url=https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/politique/legislatives-jean-luc-melenchon-n-est-pas-dans-le-paysage-politique-du-nouveau-front-populaire-dit-fabien-roussel-8238969|access-date=24 June 2024|work=France Bleu|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624073400/https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/politique/legislatives-jean-luc-melenchon-n-est-pas-dans-le-paysage-politique-du-nouveau-front-populaire-dit-fabien-roussel-8238969|url-status=live}}</ref> comments also echoed by Faure.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Blanchard|first1=François|title=Legislative: Tondelier dismisses Mélenchon and affirms that the Prime Minister will be chosen by "consensus"|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/legislatives-tondelier-ecarte-melenchon-et-affirme-que-le-premier-ministre-sera-choisi-par-consensus_AD-202406240689.html|access-date=24 June 2024|work=BFMTV|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624152413/https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/legislatives-tondelier-ecarte-melenchon-et-affirme-que-le-premier-ministre-sera-choisi-par-consensus_AD-202406240689.html|url-status=live}}</ref> Those remarks were followed by Tondelier declaring that Mélenchon would not be prime minister, and that any prime minister would have to be chosen by consensus between the forces of the New Popular Front, but she was almost immediately rebuked by LFI national coordinator [[Manuel Bompard]], who argued that "nobody can decide to exclude" Mélenchon.<ref>{{cite news|title=Mélenchon Premier ministre? Tondelier exclut l'idée et réclame un "consensus" pour Matignon|url=https://www.challenges.fr/politique/melenchon-premier-ministre-tondelier-exclut-l-idee-et-reclame-un-consensus-pour-matignon_897356|access-date=24 June 2024|work=Challenges|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630210412/https://www.challenges.fr/politique/melenchon-premier-ministre-tondelier-exclut-l-idee-et-reclame-un-consensus-pour-matignon_897356|url-status=live}}</ref> In back-to-back evening interviews on [[France 2]], [[Place Publique]] co-founder and MEP [[Raphaël Glucksmann]], echoed Tondelier's comments in declaring definitively that "Mélenchon will not be prime minister," even as Mélenchon told Hollande to "shut up" in response to his comments the previous day, complained that the speculation was due to "jealousy" of others on the left, and lamented the fact that he had to cede 100 additional constituencies to PS candidates compared to the [[New Ecological and Social People's Union]] (NUPES) in 2022 because Glucksmann's [[Party-list proportional representation|list]] outpolled the LFI list in the preceding European elections.<ref>{{cite news|title=EN DIRECT – Législatives 2024 : les programmes des «extrêmes» mènent «à la guerre civile», alerte Emmanuel Macron|url=https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/en-direct-legislatives-a-j-6-du-premier-tour-bardella-presente-le-programme-du-rn-20240624|access-date=24 June 2024|work=Le Figaro|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624063055/https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/en-direct-legislatives-a-j-6-du-premier-tour-bardella-presente-le-programme-du-rn-20240624|url-status=live}}</ref> Interviewed on 26 June, Faure said Mélenchon would not be prime minister, and the latter chided his alliance partners' "petty" bickering and reaffirmed that any decisions about who would become prime minister would only be made after the elections, but did not close the door to the possibility of him seeking the post, saying "there are those who don't like me and others who do like me."<ref name="LPFaure">{{cite news|title=DIRECT. Législatives : des appels à la retenue de l'ultradroite et l'ultragauche avant le premier tour, selon les renseignements|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/direct-legislatives-j-4-avant-le-premier-tour-au-lendemain-du-debat-entre-attal-bardella-et-bompard-26-06-2024-DZ5D4VHWZNCXNMM3225QBLRZJM.php|access-date=26 June 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=26 June 2024|archive-date=26 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240626055300/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/direct-legislatives-j-4-avant-le-premier-tour-au-lendemain-du-debat-entre-attal-bardella-et-bompard-26-06-2024-DZ5D4VHWZNCXNMM3225QBLRZJM.php|url-status=live}}</ref> On 1 July, LFI deputy [[Sophia Chikirou]] declared that "it will be either Mélenchon at Matignon, or another" LFI member if they constitute a majority of left-of-centre elected officials, owing to her feeling that other members of the alliance were indebted to them.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Maurer|first1=Pierre|last2=Duffé|first2=Julien|title=" Mélenchon, on ne peut lui faire confiance sur rien " : à gauche, le bras de fer pour le leadership continue|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/melenchon-on-ne-peut-lui-faire-confiance-sur-rien-a-gauche-le-bras-de-fer-pour-le-leadership-continue-01-07-2024-G3WDPUKVMRGYVP2YGVTN3OOJYA.php|access-date=1 July 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=1 July 2024|archive-date=1 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240701192221/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/melenchon-on-ne-peut-lui-faire-confiance-sur-rien-a-gauche-le-bras-de-fer-pour-le-leadership-continue-01-07-2024-G3WDPUKVMRGYVP2YGVTN3OOJYA.php|url-status=live}}</ref>

====Ensemble====
[[File:Gabriel Attal 2023 (cropped).jpg|thumb|left|upright|[[Gabriel Attal]] in 2023]]
The [[Together (coalition)|Ensemble]] coalition of [[Renaissance (French political party)|Renaissance]], the [[Democratic Movement (France)|Democratic Movement]] (MoDem), [[Horizons (political party)|Horizons]], the [[Union of Democrats and Independents]] (UDI), and the [[Radical Party (France)|Radical Party]] was renewed after swift negotiations soon after the [[Dissolution of parliament#France|dissolution]] announcement.<ref>{{cite news|last1=D'Angelo|first1=Robin|title=Edouard Philippe revendique davantage d'autonomie pour Horizons aux législatives 2024|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/13/legislatives-2024-edouard-philippe-revendique-davantage-d-autonomie-pour-horizons_6239420_823448.html|access-date=25 June 2024|work=Le Monde|date=13 June 2024|archive-date=23 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240623015001/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/13/legislatives-2024-edouard-philippe-revendique-davantage-d-autonomie-pour-horizons_6239420_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref><ref name="LP0625"/>

Just after the early election was called, Secretary General of Renaissance [[Stéphane Séjourné]] announced that the [[presidential majority]] would field candidates against "other republican candidates" in the hopes of splitting his opposition, with [[Clément Beaune]] naturally excluding [[La France Insoumise]] (LFI) and the [[National Rally]] (RN) from that definition.<ref name="Sejourne"/> The alliance ultimately chose not to field candidates in 67 constituencies, many of which were represented by incumbents of [[The Republicans (France)|The Republicans]] (LR), and several others from the [[Socialist Party (France)|Socialist Party]] (PS) as well as members of the [[Liberties, Independents, Overseas and Territories]] (LIOT) group in the [[National Assembly (France)|National Assembly]].<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives : 485 candidats investis par la majorité, 67 circonscriptions laissées à " l'arc républicain "|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-485-candidats-investis-par-la-majorite-67-circonscriptions-laissees-a-larc-republicain-18-06-2024-26A3Q6BOGBB2ZEBUTTPAGQBNKY.php|access-date=27 June 2024|work=Le Parisien|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=18 June 2024|archive-date=28 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240628104048/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-485-candidats-investis-par-la-majorite-67-circonscriptions-laissees-a-larc-republicain-18-06-2024-26A3Q6BOGBB2ZEBUTTPAGQBNKY.php|url-status=live}}</ref> On 12 June, [[Emmanuel Macron]] said that he had called the election to prevent a far-right victory in the [[2027 French presidential election|2027 presidential election]]. He criticised The Republicans for its potential alliance with the RN, as well as the [[New Popular Front]] (NFP), and urged all parties "able to say no to extremes" to unite.<ref>{{cite web|title=Macron says he called snap elections to prevent rise of far right in 2027 presidential vote|website=France 24|date=12 June 2024|url=https://www.france24.com/en/europe/20240612-%F0%9F%94%B4-live-france-s-macron-unveils-battle-plan-for-snap-elections|access-date=12 June 2024|archive-date=12 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240612092429/https://www.france24.com/en/europe/20240612-%F0%9F%94%B4-live-france-s-macron-unveils-battle-plan-for-snap-elections|url-status=live}}</ref>

In an open letter published on 23 June, Macron wrote that he hoped that "the future government [would gather] republicans of diverse sensibilities who will be known for their courage to oppose the extremes," in acknowledgement of the possibility of a post-election coalition. Additionally, in response to speculation that he might resign, he affirmed that he would remain president until May 2027.<ref>{{cite news|title=Emmanuel Macron s'adresse aux Français dans une lettre et promet « d'agir jusqu'en mai 2027 »|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/23/emmanuel-macron-s-adresse-aux-francais-dans-une-lettre-et-promet-d-agir-jusqu-en-mai-2027_6242970_823448.html|access-date=24 June 2024|work=Le Monde|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=23 June 2024|archive-date=23 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240623212209/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/23/emmanuel-macron-s-adresse-aux-francais-dans-une-lettre-et-promet-d-agir-jusqu-en-mai-2027_6242970_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref> Most – but not all – constitutional experts rejected the possibility of Macron resigning in order to avoid potential legislative deadlock in the event of an unclear election outcome (with legislative elections prohibited within a year of the preceding one), considering that article 6 of the [[Constitution of France|constitution]] explicitly prohibits presidents from serving more than two consecutive terms, and such a scenario would entail him seeking a third given that his current term would consider to have ended after such a resignation.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Bastuck|first1=Nicolas|title=Un troisième mandat après une démission ? " Ce serait un coup d'État ! "|url=https://www.lepoint.fr/politique/un-troisieme-mandat-apres-une-demission-ce-serait-un-coup-d-etat-11-06-2024-2562704_20.php|access-date=27 June 2024|work=Le Point|date=11 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624142116/https://www.lepoint.fr/politique/un-troisieme-mandat-apres-une-demission-ce-serait-un-coup-d-etat-11-06-2024-2562704_20.php|url-status=live}}</ref>

On 20 June, Prime Minister [[Gabriel Attal]] pledged to lower electricity bills and inheritance taxes, link pensions to inflation, and provide aid to first-time property buyers.<ref>{{cite web|title=French PM Attal pledges household finances boost ahead of legislative elections|website=France 24|date=20 June 2024|url=https://www.france24.com/en/europe/20240620-french-pm-attal-pledges-household-finances-boost-ahead-of-legislative-elections|access-date=20 June 2024|archive-date=20 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240620102821/https://www.france24.com/en/europe/20240620-french-pm-attal-pledges-household-finances-boost-ahead-of-legislative-elections|url-status=live}}</ref> Other proposals he presented included raising the value-sharing bonus by up to €10,000 per year, constructing 14 new nuclear reactors, banning access to social networks to those aged 15 and under, halving the usage of pesticides by 2030, and doubling the army budget by 2030.<ref>{{cite news|title=Élections législatives 2024 : le programme de Gabriel Attal et d'Ensemble, la coalition présidentielle|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/elections-legislatives-2024-le-programme-de-gabriel-attal-et-d-ensemble-la-coalition-presidentielle_AV-202406270030.html|access-date=27 June 2024|work=BFMTV|date=27 June 2024|archive-date=27 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240627035826/https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/elections-legislatives-2024-le-programme-de-gabriel-attal-et-d-ensemble-la-coalition-presidentielle_AV-202406270030.html|url-status=live}}</ref> Echoing the RN's proposals in response to a spate of youth violence, Attal also announced that he would seek to abolish age as a mitigating circumstance for statutory penalties by default, meaning that judges would charge lawbreaking children as adults unless they provided explanations as to why an exception should be granted. At the same time, he attacked the RN's programme of "division, hate, and stigmatisation," and said the RN's backtracking on various economic policies showed that they were "not ready to govern."<ref>{{cite news|last1=Boichot|first1=Loris|last2=Quinault-Maupoil|first2=Tristan|last3=Trémolet de Villers|first3=Vincent|title=Gabriel Attal au Figaro : "Le pays joue sa peau"|url=https://www.lefigaro.fr/politique/gabriel-attal-au-figaro-le-pays-joue-sa-peau-20240624|access-date=24 June 2024|work=Le Figaro|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624215241/https://www.lefigaro.fr/politique/gabriel-attal-au-figaro-le-pays-joue-sa-peau-20240624|url-status=live}}</ref> Macron likewise castigated the "uninhibited racism or anti-Semitism" of the campaign in response to RN deputy [[Roger Chudeau]] saying that his fellow former cabinet member [[Najat Vallaud-Belkacem]] should not have been able to serve because of her dual nationality.<ref>{{cite news|title=En direct, législatives 2024 : des manifestations contre le RN et l'extrême droite ont eu lieu dans plusieurs grandes villes de France|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/06/27/en-direct-legislatives-2024-pendant-le-debat-olivier-faure-defend-une-relance-economique-par-la-demande-gabriel-attal-estime-que-de-fortes-hausses-de-salaires-couteraient-trop-cher-aux-entreprises_6244426_823448.html|access-date=28 June 2024|work=Le Monde|date=27 June 2024|archive-date=27 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240627215912/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/06/27/en-direct-legislatives-2024-pendant-le-debat-olivier-faure-defend-une-relance-economique-par-la-demande-gabriel-attal-estime-que-de-fortes-hausses-de-salaires-couteraient-trop-cher-aux-entreprises_6244426_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

Trailing in third place nationally behind the NFP and RN in pre-election polls, Macron and his allies decided to focus their attacks on the programme of the New Popular Front prior to the first round and mostly avoid direct confrontation against the RN until the second round.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Gatinois|first1=Claire|title=La stratégie court-termiste d'Emmanuel Macron : attaquer la gauche et reporter la confrontation contre le RN au second tour|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/20/emmanuel-macron-pilonne-la-gauche-et-reporte-au-second-tour-la-bataille-contre-le-rn_6241516_823448.html|access-date=20 June 2024|work=Le Monde|date=20 June 2024|archive-date=20 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240620035226/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/20/emmanuel-macron-pilonne-la-gauche-et-reporte-au-second-tour-la-bataille-contre-le-rn_6241516_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref> Attal claimed that the NFP's proposal to raise the minimum wage by 14.3% to net €1,600 per month would lead to the loss of 500,000 jobs, and [[Ministry of Economics and Finance (France)|Minister of Finance]] [[Bruno Le Maire]] claimed that it would be "a catastrophe" resulting in "mass unemployment" if implemented, with the [[European Commission]] having just announced it would meet to launch the excessive deficit procedure against France.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Marotte|first1=Thibault|title=Les dangers du Smic à 1 600 euros : "Ce ne serait pas un coup de pouce mais un coup de poing"|url=https://www.lexpress.fr/economie/les-dangers-du-smic-a-1-600-euros-ce-ne-serait-pas-un-coup-de-pouce-mais-un-coup-de-poing-LR2YCLLDWRCVBO64QJFWZXSANA/|access-date=24 June 2024|work=L'Express|date=22 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624025631/https://www.lexpress.fr/economie/les-dangers-du-smic-a-1-600-euros-ce-ne-serait-pas-un-coup-de-pouce-mais-un-coup-de-poing-LR2YCLLDWRCVBO64QJFWZXSANA/|url-status=live}}</ref> Macron publicly denounced the NFP's "totally immigrationist" stance and decried proposals which would make it easier for transgender people to change their civil status by allowing them to do so at their local town hall as "completely grotesque,"<ref>{{cite news|title=Macron cible la gauche et brouille les pistes|url=https://www.challenges.fr/politique/macron-cible-la-gauche-et-brouille-les-pistes_896842|access-date=21 June 2024|work=Challenges|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=19 June 2024|archive-date=21 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240621061855/https://www.challenges.fr/politique/macron-cible-la-gauche-et-brouille-les-pistes_896842|url-status=live}}</ref> and his former prime minister [[Élisabeth Borne]] decried the alliance as being one of "separatist wokists who support Islamism and communitarianism" with a nonsensical programme and disastrous economic policies.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Quinault-Maupoil|first1=Tristan|title="J'ai quelques idées sur ce qui peut être utile pour le pays..." Élisabeth Borne, à quitte ou double dans le Calvados|url=https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/j-ai-quelques-idees-sur-ce-qui-peut-etre-utile-pour-le-pays-elisabeth-borne-a-quitte-ou-double-dans-le-calvados-20240620|access-date=21 June 2024|work=Le Figaro|date=20 June 2024|archive-date=20 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240620122115/https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/j-ai-quelques-idees-sur-ce-qui-peut-etre-utile-pour-le-pays-elisabeth-borne-a-quitte-ou-double-dans-le-calvados-20240620|url-status=live}}</ref>

A recurring theme of the Ensemble campaign was the willingness of its figureheads to draw equivalencies between the New Popular Front and National Rally. On 21 June, Macron argued that, "contrary to what some say," the left and RN are not "rampart[s] of [each] other ... there are extremes we must not allow to pass."<ref>{{cite news|title=Macron renvoie dos à dos les extrêmes et appelle à voter contre|url=https://www.lepoint.fr/politique/macron-renvoie-dos-a-dos-les-extremes-et-appelle-a-voter-contre-21-06-2024-2563606_20.php|access-date=21 June 2024|work=Le Point|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=21 June 2024|archive-date=21 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240621205034/https://www.lepoint.fr/politique/macron-renvoie-dos-a-dos-les-extremes-et-appelle-a-voter-contre-21-06-2024-2563606_20.php|url-status=live}}</ref> Finance minister Bruno Le Maire warned that a victory by either the far-right or the left could cause a financial crisis,<ref name="bbcfront"/> lambasting both of their economic platforms as "leftist projects inspired by Marxism."<ref>{{cite news|last1=Chicheportiche|first1=Olivier|title=Pour Bruno Le Maire, les programmes économiques du Nouveau Front populaire et du RN sont "marxistes"|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/economie/economie-social/france/pour-bruno-le-maire-les-programmes-economiques-du-nouveau-front-populaire-et-du-rn-sont-marxistes_AV-202406240339.html|access-date=25 June 2024|work=BFMTV|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=25 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240625031246/https://www.bfmtv.com/economie/economie-social/france/pour-bruno-le-maire-les-programmes-economiques-du-nouveau-front-populaire-et-du-rn-sont-marxistes_AV-202406240339.html|url-status=live}}</ref> In an interview on 24 June, [[Minister for Gender Equality, Diversity and Equal Opportunities|Gender Equality Minister]] [[Aurore Bergé]] remarked that "the best rampart, particularly against the Popular Front, is not the RN, it's us," and like Macron, refused to give second-round voting instructions in support of either of "the extremes" represented by the New Popular Front and RN prior to the first round.<ref name="Berge">{{cite news|title=DIRECT. Législatives: Attal estime que le RN et LFI s'"alimentent" avec "des discours de division"|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/direct-legislatives-la-campagne-entre-dans-sa-derniere-ligne-droite-apres-la-lettre-d-emmanuel-macron-le-rn-presente-son-programme_LN-202406240059.html|access-date=24 June 2024|work=BFMTV|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624044849/https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/direct-legislatives-la-campagne-entre-dans-sa-derniere-ligne-droite-apres-la-lettre-d-emmanuel-macron-le-rn-presente-son-programme_LN-202406240059.html|url-status=live}}</ref> In a podcast episode released the same day, Macron warned that the "two extremes" would lead France "to civil war," whether because of the xenophobia of the RN or the communitarianism of the left.<ref>{{cite news|title=Les programmes des "extrêmes" mènent "à la guerre civile", alerte Macron|url=https://www.lexpress.fr/politique/melenchon-ne-sera-pas-premier-ministre-assure-la-patronne-des-ecologistes-marine-tondelier-WCGPCJWQTVFV3IRC5LSAHVBJ7E/|access-date=24 June 2024|work=L'Express|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624145444/https://www.lexpress.fr/politique/melenchon-ne-sera-pas-premier-ministre-assure-la-patronne-des-ecologistes-marine-tondelier-WCGPCJWQTVFV3IRC5LSAHVBJ7E/|url-status=live}}</ref>

Many of Macron's closest advisors publicly expressed dismay at his decision to dissolve the National Assembly in the days after his surprise announcement. [[Yaël Braun-Pivet]], [[president of the National Assembly of France|president of the National Assembly]] before the dissolution, privately disagreed with the decision and attempted to dissuade him, and said she believed that a coalition was possible. Finance Minister Bruno Le Maire trashed Macron's coterie at the Élysée as "woodlice," and his former prime minister [[Édouard Philippe]], head of the Horizons party within the Ensemble alliance, said that Macron had "killed the presidential majority" through his reckless decision.<ref name="YBP">{{cite news|last1=Septier|first1=Hugo|title=Philippe, Le Maire, Braun-Pivet... Ces cadres de la macronie affichent leur rupture avec le président après la dissolution|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/la-republique-en-marche/philippe-le-maire-braun-pivet-ces-cadres-de-la-macronie-affichent-leur-rupture-avec-le-president-apres-la-dissolution_AN-202406210346.html|access-date=24 June 2024|work=BFMTV|date=21 June 2024|archive-date=22 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240622222101/https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/la-republique-en-marche/philippe-le-maire-braun-pivet-ces-cadres-de-la-macronie-affichent-leur-rupture-avec-le-president-apres-la-dissolution_AN-202406210346.html|url-status=live}}</ref> Outgoing Ensemble deputies expressed exasperation with Macron, with one remarking that "I wish he'd shut up and let us get out of the mess he's gotten us into;" [[François Bayrou]], leader of alliance member MoDem, deemed it necessary to "de-Macronise the campaign;"<ref>{{cite news|last1=Théveniaud|first1=Pauline|last2=Beaumont|first2=Olivier|title=" Je ne me préoccupe plus de ce que dit le président ! " : la stratégie électorale de Macron choque son camp|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/je-ne-me-preoccupe-plus-de-ce-que-dit-le-president-la-strategie-electorale-de-macron-choque-son-camp-19-06-2024-2CUWWGPB6RGX5HXNM2RDYTZEMI.php|access-date=24 June 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=19 June 2024|archive-date=21 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240621103954/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/je-ne-me-preoccupe-plus-de-ce-que-dit-le-president-la-strategie-electorale-de-macron-choque-son-camp-19-06-2024-2CUWWGPB6RGX5HXNM2RDYTZEMI.php|url-status=live}}</ref> and candidates became "fed up" with Macron's refusal to abide by his promise to stay out of the campaign.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Théveniaud|first1=Pauline|title=" Il ne peut pas s'en empêcher " : à l'approche du premier tour, Emmanuel Macron ne baisse pas le son|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/il-ne-peut-pas-sen-empecher-a-lapproche-du-premier-tour-emmanuel-macron-ne-baisse-pas-le-son-24-06-2024-RLYMYWOM5BAUFIO7AQPYFOW5MM.php|access-date=25 June 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=25 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240625000831/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/il-ne-peut-pas-sen-empecher-a-lapproche-du-premier-tour-emmanuel-macron-ne-baisse-pas-le-son-24-06-2024-RLYMYWOM5BAUFIO7AQPYFOW5MM.php|url-status=live}}</ref>

As Macron's popularity ratings plunged to their lowest level ever in post-dissolution surveys, with {{ill|Frédéric Dabi|fr}} noting that most respondents in an [[Institut français d'opinion publique|Ifop]]-[[Le Journal du Dimanche|JDD]] survey characterised the decision as "incomprehensible," "thoughtless," or "irresponsible" and 70% in a BVA Xsight-[[RTL (French radio)|RTL]] survey declaring that they did not want Macron involved in the campaign,<ref>{{cite news|last1=André|first1=Antonin|title=SONDAGE – Les Français de plus en plus mécontents d'Emmanuel Macron|url=https://www.lejdd.fr/politique/sondage-les-francais-de-plus-en-plus-mecontents-demmanuel-macron-146678|access-date=24 June 2024|work=Le Journal du Dimanche|date=23 June 2024|archive-date=23 news|title=INFO RTL – La cote de popularité d'Emmanuel Macron s'effondre après la dissolution de l'Assemblée, selon notre candidates kept a local focus, with images of Macron were almost entirely absent from campaign posters: only one out of 22 government ministers' posters featured his image.<ref>{{cite Along with Philippe, Le Maire, and [[Minister of the Interior (France)|Minister of the Interior]] [[Gérald Darmanin]] (who announced that he would leave the government if re-elected to the National many of Macron's early supporters distanced themselves from him,<ref>{{cite news|title=Ferrand, Castaner, Castex… Le blues des premiers compagnons de route de Macron|url=https://www.letelegramme.fr/elections/legislatives/ferrand-castaner-castex-le-blues-des-premiers-compagnons-de-route-de-macron-6612262.php|access-date=26 June 2024|work=Le ====The Republicans====
[[File:Éric Ciotti (cropped).jpg|thumb|upright|[[Éric Ciotti]] in 2023]]
{{Main|2024 The Republicans crisis|Union of the Far-Right}}
The president of [[The Republicans (France)|The Republicans]] (LR), [[Éric Ciotti]], spoke in favour of an alliance with the [[National Rally]] (RN) during an 11 June interview with the French channel [[TF1]]. [[Olivier Marleix]], the head of the party in the [[National Assembly (France)|National Assembly]], called for Ciotti's resignation in response.<ref name=":0">{{cite web|title=France's Republicans leader wants to form 'alliance' with Le Pen's NR|website=Al Jazeera|date=11 June 2024|url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/6/11/frances-republicans-leader-wants-to-form-alliance-with-le-pens-nr|access-date=11 June 2024|archive-date=11 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240611185401/https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2024/6/11/frances-republicans-leader-wants-to-form-alliance-with-le-pens-nr|url-status=live}}</ref> On 12 June, The Republicans' political committee voted unanimously to remove Ciotti as its president and expel him from the party. However, the latter rejected the decision, calling it "a flagrant violation of our statutes" that was illegal and void.<ref name=f2412june>{{cite web|title=France's rightwing Les Républicains vote out leader Éric Ciotti over election pact with far right|website=France 24|date=12 June 2024|url=https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20240612-%F0%9F%94%B4-france-s-rightwing-les-r%C3%A9publicains-vote-out-leader-%C3%A9ric-ciotti-over-election-pact-with-far-right|access-date=26 June 2024|archive-date=27 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240627024429/https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20240612-%F0%9F%94%B4-france-s-rightwing-les-r%C3%A9publicains-vote-out-leader-%C3%A9ric-ciotti-over-election-pact-with-far-right|url-status=live}}</ref> A Paris court reviewed the decision on 14 June, in which Ciotti was reinstated as party leader in the interim, as well as a member of the party,<ref>{{Cite web|date=14 June 2024|title=Court suspends French right-wing leader Ciotti's expulsion from party|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/en/politics/article/2024/06/14/court-suspends-french-right-wing-leader-ciotti-s-expulsion-from-party_6674830_5.html|access-date=14 June 2024|website=Le Monde|archive-date=14 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240614182631/https://www.lemonde.fr/en/politics/article/2024/06/14/court-suspends-french-right-wing-leader-ciotti-s-expulsion-from-party_6674830_5.html|url-status=live}}</ref> which was followed by two additional abortive attempts to remove him,<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives : la justice rejette la troisième tentative de LR d'exclure Éric Ciotti|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-la-justice-rejette-la-troisieme-tentative-de-lr-dexclure-eric-ciotti-27-06-2024-K2JEKB6PURF5RBS26IXTOTWD4U.php|access-date=27 June 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=27 June 2024|archive-date=27 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240627170014/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-la-justice-rejette-la-troisieme-tentative-de-lr-dexclure-eric-ciotti-27-06-2024-K2JEKB6PURF5RBS26IXTOTWD4U.php|url-status=live}}</ref> while the local branch of The Republicans in [[Hauts-de-Seine]] announced a local alliance with [[Renaissance (French political party)|Renaissance]].<ref name="bbcfront"/> On 17 June, Ciotti secured an agreement with RN to present 62 candidates (later 63), none of which are outgoing LR deputies except for himself and his close ally [[Christelle d'Intorni]], while the national investiture committee of LR unveiled candidates in a majority of other constituencies, including all other incumbent deputies seeking re-election, as well as fielding candidates against both Ciotti and d'Intorni.<ref name="CNILR">{{cite news|last1=Guez|first1=Ariel|title=Législatives: au moins 62 candidats soutenus par Éric Ciotti et le RN, près de 400 par Les Républicains|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/legislatives-au-moins-62-candidats-soutenus-par-eric-ciotti-et-le-rn-pres-de-400-par-les-republicains_AV-202406170053.html|access-date=20 June 2024|work=BFMTV|date=17 June 2024|archive-date=20 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240620060649/https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/legislatives-au-moins-62-candidats-soutenus-par-eric-ciotti-et-le-rn-pres-de-400-par-les-republicains_AV-202406170053.html|url-status=live}}</ref><ref name="CNI"/><ref name="LM1"/> Because Ciotti requested that the party's bank require his authorisation for any transactions, LR candidates are not receiving any financial support from the party.<ref>{{cite news|title=En direct, législatives 2024 : François Hollande souhaite un « désistement républicain » face au RN, Jean-Luc Mélenchon appelle à ne pas faire la « bêtise » de voter pour l'extrême droite|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/06/26/en-direct-legislatives-2024-il-n-y-a-pas-d-economiste-serieux-defendant-le-programme-economique-du-rn-celui-ci-est-tres-evolutif-donc-sans-logique-ideologique_6243809_823448.html|access-date=26 June 2024|work=Le Monde|date=26 June 2024|archive-date=26 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240626135731/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/06/26/en-direct-legislatives-2024-il-n-y-a-pas-d-economiste-serieux-defendant-le-programme-economique-du-rn-celui-ci-est-tres-evolutif-donc-sans-logique-ideologique_6243809_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

With no detailed national election programme to run on, most LR candidates opted to campaign primarily on issues concerning their constituencies, rely on their strong local roots and name recognition in order to fight for their survival, and keep their distance from the drama surrounding the other three main political forces and Ciotti's alliance with the RN. Numerous incumbent LR deputies declined to feature the party's logo on their election paraphernalia, stayed out of national media, and tried to portray themselves as independent of any party, with [[Aurélien Pradié]] choosing to describe himself on leaflets as "a strong voice, a free voice,"<ref name="LRLE">{{cite news|last1=Legavre-Jérôme|first1=Ulysse|title=Législatives 2024 : les candidats LR misent sur leur implantation locale pour sauver leur siège|url=https://www.lesechos.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-2024-les-candidats-lr-misent-sur-leur-implantation-locale-pour-sauver-leur-siege-2103071|access-date=25 June 2024|work=Les Echos|date=21 June 2024|archive-date=25 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240625035536/https://www.lesechos.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-2024-les-candidats-lr-misent-sur-leur-implantation-locale-pour-sauver-leur-siege-2103071|url-status=live}}</ref> before announcing that he would run only under the label of his micro-party ''Du courage'' on 26 June, declaring in an interview with ''[[La Dépêche du Midi|La Dépêche]]'' that "[[Gaullism]] isn't dead, it's more alive than ever, but LR is dead."<ref>{{cite news|last1=Bertoni|first1=Laetitia|last2=Bousquet|first2=Gil|title=EXCLUSIF. Législatives 2024 – Aurélien Pradié quitte LR : "Le parti auquel j'appartenais n'est plus capable de parler aux Français"|url=https://www.ladepeche.fr/2024/06/26/elections-legislatives-le-parti-auquel-jappartenais-nest-plus-capable-de-parler-aux-francais-declare-aurelien-pradie-en-claquant-la-porte-des-12039418.php|access-date=26 June 2024|work=La Dépêche|date=26 June 2024|archive-date=26 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240626055330/https://www.ladepeche.fr/2024/06/26/elections-legislatives-le-parti-auquel-jappartenais-nest-plus-capable-de-parler-aux-francais-declare-aurelien-pradie-en-claquant-la-porte-des-12039418.php|url-status=live}}</ref> This reduced visibility was also the product of the highly varied circumstances of LR candidates, with 63 invested as part of the LR-RN alliance, roughly 400 invested by the party's national investiture committee, and 39 other candidates (including 26 incumbents) completely unopposed by the [[Together (coalition)|Ensemble]] coalition owing to their "constructive" alignment with Macron's policies. Even figures with a significant national profile like former party president [[Laurent Wauquiez]], threatened by the possibility of an RN wave, sought to stay out of the national spotlight and focused on avoiding being subsumed by the tripolarisation of the electorate.<ref name="LRLE"/><ref name="LM1"/>

====National Rally====
[[File:Jordan Bardella (cropped).jpg|thumb|upright|[[Jordan Bardella]] in 2022]]
Eight of the 30 [[National Rally]] (RN) [[Member of the European Parliament|MEP]]s newly elected to the [[European Parliament]] in June 2024 decided to run in the national election. As occupying both posts is impossible, MEPs who won in the legislative elections were replaced with other party members further down the [[Party-list proportional representation|list]].<ref>{{cite magazine|magazine=Marianne|title=Tout juste élus le 9 juin, près d'un tiers des eurodéputés RN candidats aux législatives|first=Constantin|last=Gaschignard|date=18 June 2024|url=https://www.marianne.net/politique/tout-juste-elus-le-9-juin-pres-dun-tiers-des-eurodeputes-rn-candidats-aux-legislatives|lang=fr|access-date=23 June 2024|archive-date=19 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240619090710/https://www.marianne.net/politique/tout-juste-elus-le-9-juin-pres-dun-tiers-des-eurodeputes-rn-candidats-aux-legislatives|url-status=live}}</ref>
 
[[Marine Le Pen]] promised that the RN would form a "national unity government" should it win the election,<ref name="France24">{{Cite news|date=14 June 2024|title=French left-wing alliance New Popular Front vows 'total break' with Macron policies|url=https://www.france24.com/en/europe/20240614-french-leftwing-alliance-new-popular-front-vows-to-break-with-macron-policies|access-date=14 June 2024|website=France 24|language=en|archive-date=14 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240614125405/https://www.france24.com/en/europe/20240614-french-leftwing-alliance-new-popular-front-vows-to-break-with-macron-policies|url-status=live}}</ref> and in an interview with ''[[La Voix du Nord]]'', she indicated she was open to the possibility of appointments for figures from the left in an RN-led government.<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives : en cas de majorité absolue, Bardella promet d'être le Premier ministre de " tous les Français "|url=https://www.sudouest.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-en-cas-de-majorite-absolue-bardella-promet-d-etre-le-premier-ministre-de-tous-les-francais-20251250.php|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Sud Ouest|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=22 June 2024|archive-date=22 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240622203818/https://www.sudouest.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-en-cas-de-majorite-absolue-bardella-promet-d-etre-le-premier-ministre-de-tous-les-francais-20251250.php|url-status=live}}</ref> At the same time, party leader [[Jordan Bardella]] said that he was "the only one capable of blocking [[Jean-Luc Mélenchon]] and blocking the far left" and urged "all the patriotic forces of the republic" to unite and prevent the left from winning the election. He also pledged to pass an immigration law allowing the deportation of "delinquents and Islamists" and cut energy costs as prime minister.<ref name="bbcfront">{{Cite news|date=14 June 2024|title=French left forms 'popular front' to fight far right|url=https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c6ppjvq5jv1o|access-date=21 June 2024|website=BBC|language=en|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630221012/https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c6ppjvq5jv1o|url-status=live}}</ref> In an interview with ''[[Le Monde]]'', Le Pen confirmed that Bardella would not seek the post of prime minister in the absence of an absolute majority.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Guillou|first1=Clément|title=" On ne s'interdit rien " : les plans de Marine Le Pen en cas de victoire de l'extrême droite aux législatives|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/20/on-ne-s-interdit-rien-les-plans-de-marine-le-pen-en-cas-de-victoire-aux-elections-legislatives_6241755_823448.html|access-date=21 June 2024|work=Le Monde|date=20 June 2024|archive-date=21 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240621011157/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/20/on-ne-s-interdit-rien-les-plans-de-marine-le-pen-en-cas-de-victoire-aux-elections-legislatives_6241755_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

On 18 June, Bardella urged voters to give his party an "absolute majority" for it to be able to govern effectively, while pledging to cut energy taxes to 5.5% from 20%.<ref>{{Cite news|date=18 June 2024|title=French left forms 'popular front' to fight far right|url=https://www.france24.com/en/france/20240618-far-right-leader-bardella-says-he-needs-absolute-majority-to-govern-france-effectively|access-date=18 June 2024|website=France 24|language=en|archive-date=18 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240618104426/https://www.france24.com/en/france/20240618-far-right-leader-bardella-says-he-needs-absolute-majority-to-govern-france-effectively|url-status=live}}</ref> Bardella pledged to uphold French military commitments to [[NATO]] and [[Russian invasion of Ukraine|support Ukraine against the Russian invasion]], but ruled out sending long-range missiles and other weapons that could be used to strike Russian territory.<ref>{{cite news|title=France's far-right Bardella says he backs Ukraine but wouldn't send missiles that could hit Russia|url=https://www.france24.com/en/france/20240619-france-s-far-right-bardella-says-he-backs-ukraine-but-won-t-send-missiles-that-could-hit-russia|access-date=24 June 2024|work=France 24|date=19 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624023719/https://www.france24.com/en/france/20240619-france-s-far-right-bardella-says-he-backs-ukraine-but-won-t-send-missiles-that-could-hit-russia|url-status=live}}</ref> Alluding to the possibility of [[Emmanuel Macron]] sending ground forces to Ukraine, Le Pen deemed Macron's title of "commander-in-chief of the armed forces" as "honorary" given the need for both the heads and state and government to make most defence decisions, though constitutional law experts noted that the president's approval was still required for the usage of nuclear weapons.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Berrod|first1=Nicolas|title=Emmanuel Macron, chef des armées " honorifique " ? Ce que dit vraiment la Constitution|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/politique/emmanuel-macron-chef-des-armees-honorifique-ce-que-dit-vraiment-la-constitution-27-06-2024-UGWD6MIKY5DU3NMH6JGFDWYGYE.php|access-date=27 June 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=27 June 2024|archive-date=27 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240627094658/https://www.leparisien.fr/politique/emmanuel-macron-chef-des-armees-honorifique-ce-que-dit-vraiment-la-constitution-27-06-2024-UGWD6MIKY5DU3NMH6JGFDWYGYE.php|url-status=live}}</ref>

Due to worries about public backlash and concerns from investors, the RN softened and postponed some elements of its initial economic proposals, including the planned tax exemptions on those under 30 and abolition of the [[value-added tax]] (VAT) on 100 essential products,<ref>{{cite news|last1=Guillou|first1=Clément|last2=Lesueur|first2=Corentin|title=Législatives 2024 : comment le RN écrit le récit de son empêchement en cas de victoire|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/14/legislatives-2024-comment-le-rn-ecrit-le-recit-de-son-empechement-en-cas-de-victoire_6239930_823448.html|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Le Monde|date=14 June 2024|archive-date=22 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240622001021/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/14/legislatives-2024-comment-le-rn-ecrit-le-recit-de-son-empechement-en-cas-de-victoire_6239930_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref> and proposals to increase teachers' salaries were also deferred. Despite initial claims otherwise, Bardella reaffirmed on 17 June that the RN intended to repeal the [[2023 French pension reform law|2023 pension reform]] and reduce the legal retirement age to 60, but only for those who started working before the age of 20.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Horn|first1=Alexandre|last2=Quenescourt|first2=Enzo|title=Réforme des retraites, fiscalité, augmentation des salaires des profs : la liste des renoncements du RN avant les législatives s'allonge|url=https://www.liberation.fr/checknews/reforme-des-retraites-fiscalite-augmentation-des-salaires-des-profs-la-liste-des-renoncements-du-rn-avant-les-legislatives-sallonge-20240618_2IUKWPAC6VBZ7HKX7QHHIK42RA/|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Libération|date=18 June 2024|archive-date=19 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240619021132/https://www.liberation.fr/checknews/reforme-des-retraites-fiscalite-augmentation-des-salaires-des-profs-la-liste-des-renoncements-du-rn-avant-les-legislatives-sallonge-20240618_2IUKWPAC6VBZ7HKX7QHHIK42RA/|url-status=live}}</ref> In an interview with ''[[Le Journal du Dimanche]]'' published on 22 June, Bardella announced that, as prime minister, he would initiate a national budgetary audit and call a constitutional referendum to guarantee reductions in migratory flows in 2027. He also stated that he did not support [[Frexit]] and assured that, after their alliance, members of [[The Republicans (France)|The Republicans]] (LR) supported jointly by [[Éric Ciotti]] and the RN would be included in his government.<ref>{{cite news|last1=André|first1=Antonin|last2=Torres|first2=Jules|last3=Lejeune|first3=Geoffroy|title=EXCLUSIF – Jordan Bardella au JDD : " L'histoire s'accélère et je crois que nous pouvons gagner "|url=https://www.lejdd.fr/politique/exclusif-jordan-bardella-au-jdd-lhistoire-saccelere-et-je-crois-que-nous-pouvons-gagner-146669|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Le Journal du Dimanche|date=22 June 2024|archive-date=23 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240623090606/https://www.lejdd.fr/politique/exclusif-jordan-bardella-au-jdd-lhistoire-saccelere-et-je-crois-que-nous-pouvons-gagner-146669|url-status=live}}</ref>

Bardella officially unveiled the RN's programme on 24 June, including measures to introduce [[mandatory sentencing]], end [[child benefit]]s for parents of underage repeat offenders, and sentence youth criminals to short prison sentences at closed educational centres for children. He confirmed that the RN continued to intend to abolish ''[[jus soli]]'' because "the automatic acquisition of French nationality is no longer justified in a world of 8 billion people, [with] our daily struggles of our inability to integrate and assimilate them multiplying on our soil," and expressed his desire to both "re-establish the offence of illegal stays" and solidify these proposals in the constitution "to also make them untouchable by European or international jurisprudence" through a national referendum. In addition, he declared that he would scrutinise "spending that encourages immigration" and "certain expensive and abusive tax loopholes," and that the reversal of Macron's pension reform would be implemented gradually, shifting the legal retirement age to 62 for those who have worked for at least 40 years.<ref name="RN2"/> The party is against measures to tackle climate change and protecting the environment.<ref>{{Cite news|date=20 June 2024|title=French elections: Why is the rejection of environmentalism a driving force behind France's far-right vote?|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/en/environment/article/2024/06/20/french-elections-why-is-the-rejection-of-environmentalism-a-driving-force-behind-france-s-far-right-vote_6675235_114.html|access-date=30 June 2024|work=Le Monde.fr|language=en|archive-date=29 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240629145400/https://www.lemonde.fr/en/environment/article/2024/06/20/french-elections-why-is-the-rejection-of-environmentalism-a-driving-force-behind-france-s-far-right-vote_6675235_114.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

Other RN proposals included seeking to provide incentives for medical professionals to work in underserved areas and for retirees to return to work,<ref name="RN2">{{cite news|title=Législatives 2024 : "big bang de l'autorité" à l'école, suppression du droit du sol... Jordan Bardella a présenté le programme du RN|url=https://www.francetvinfo.fr/politique/front-national/legislatives-2024-big-bang-de-l-autorite-a-l-ecole-suppression-du-droit-du-sol-jordan-bardella-a-presente-le-programme-pour-le-rn_6623139.html|access-date=24 June 2024|work=franceinfo|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624123651/https://www.francetvinfo.fr/politique/front-national/legislatives-2024-big-bang-de-l-autorite-a-l-ecole-suppression-du-droit-du-sol-jordan-bardella-a-presente-le-programme-pour-le-rn_6623139.html|url-status=live}}</ref> reducing taxes on agriculture, privatising French national media, boosting fertility rates by allowing parents to claim their first two children as a full share rather than the current half-share for the purposes of personal income tax calculations, eliminating inheritance taxes for lower-income families, continuing to not [[International recognition of the State of Palestine|recognise Palestine as a state]] as doing so would, in his view, be "to recognise terrorism,"<ref>{{cite news|last1=Sdiri|first1=Noah|title=Droit du sol, retraites, natalité… Le RN dévoile les grands axes de son programme|url=https://www.lejdd.fr/politique/droit-du-sol-retraites-natalite-le-rn-devoile-les-grands-axes-de-son-programme-146739|access-date=24 June 2024|work=Le Journal du Dimanche|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624132550/https://www.lejdd.fr/politique/droit-du-sol-retraites-natalite-le-rn-devoile-les-grands-axes-de-son-programme-146739|url-status=live}}</ref> imposing moratoriums on new wind farms and the closure of healthcare facilities, banning agricultural products which fall below standards for domestic products, and ensuring that only French nationals be eligible for some security and defence jobs, after an earlier announcement that [[Multiple citizenship|Dual nationals]] would be banned from such "sensitive" jobs as those.<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives 2024 : ce qu'il faut retenir du programme du RN présenté par Jordan Bardella|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/24/ce-qu-il-faut-retenir-du-programme-du-rn-presente-par-jordan-bardella_6243369_823448.html|access-date=24 June 2024|work=Le Monde|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624121259/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/24/ce-qu-il-faut-retenir-du-programme-du-rn-presente-par-jordan-bardella_6243369_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref> After outcry following RN deputy [[Roger Chudeau]]'s comments that dual nationals (specifically [[Najat Vallaud-Belkacem]]) should not hold ministerial posts, Le Pen disavowed the idea that of restricting ministerial posts on basis of dual nationality and added that Chudeau's comments were contrary to the RN's programme.<ref>{{cite news|title=Marine Le Pen désavoue un député RN après ses critiques sur la binationalité de Najat Vallaud-Belkacem|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/28/marine-le-pen-desavoue-un-depute-rn-apres-ses-critiques-sur-la-binationalite-de-najat-vallaud-belkacem_6245012_823448.html|access-date=28 June 2024|work=Le Monde|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=28 June 2024|archive-date=28 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240628091640/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/06/28/marine-le-pen-desavoue-un-depute-rn-apres-ses-critiques-sur-la-binationalite-de-najat-vallaud-belkacem_6245012_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

====Other political parties====

[[Marion Maréchal]], a far-right candidate for [[Reconquête]] in the [[2024 European Parliament election in France|preceding European Parliament election]], met with her aunt [[Marine Le Pen]] and [[Jordan Bardella]], leaders of the [[National Rally]] (RN), on 10 June in order to discuss a potential far-right alliance during the legislative election.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.politico.eu/article/french-far-right-jordan-bardella-president-emmanuel-macron-election-european-election-national-rally/|title=France's conservatives and far right explore uniting to beat Macron|website=[[Politico]]|last=Goury-Laffont|first=Victor|access-date=12 June 2024|date=10 June 2024|archive-date=11 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240611222436/https://www.politico.eu/article/french-far-right-jordan-bardella-president-emmanuel-macron-election-european-election-national-rally/|url-status=live}}</ref> After the meeting, Maréchal indicated that Bardella was opposed to an alliance with Reconquête as his party did not want to be affiliated with Reconquête party leader [[Éric Zemmour]];<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.politico.eu/article/french-far-right-alliance-talks-break-down-controversial-figure-eric-zemmour-marine-le-pen/|title=French far-right alliance talks break down|website=[[Politico]]|last=Goury-Laffont|first=Victor|access-date=12 June 2024|date=11 June 2024|archive-date=11 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240611175846/https://www.politico.eu/article/french-far-right-alliance-talks-break-down-controversial-figure-eric-zemmour-marine-le-pen/|url-status=live}}</ref> regardless, she announced her endorsement of the RN. On 12 June, Zemmour announced that he was expelling Maréchal from the party.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.france24.com/en/video/20240613-far-right-reconquest-founder-zemmour-expels-mar%C3%A9chal-from-party|title=Far-right Reconquest founder Zemmour expels Maréchal from party|website=[[France 24]]|access-date=13 June 2024|date=13 June 2024|archive-date=13 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240613142133/https://www.france24.com/en/video/20240613-far-right-reconquest-founder-zemmour-expels-mar%C3%A9chal-from-party|url-status=live}}</ref> The party ultimately presented candidates in 330 constituencies, deciding not to run candidates in constituencies where ideologically similar candidates had the strongest chance of winning.<ref name="Rec1"/>

[[Debout la France]] only contested 107 constituencies, backing candidates supported by the RN elsewhere, and party leader [[Nicolas Dupont-Aignan]] expressed his support for the alliance between [[Éric Ciotti]] and the RN.<ref name="DLF1"/><ref name="DLF2"/>

Trotskyist party [[Lutte Ouvrière]] presented candidates in 550 constituencies. Other parties presenting a double-digit number of candidates, according to a ''[[Le Monde]]'' analysis, include the [[New Anticapitalist Party]] with 30 candidates, [[Ecology at the Centre]] with 23 candidates, [[Unser Land]] with 14 candidates, and [[Résistons!]] with 12 candidates.<ref name="LM1"/> The [[Animalist Party]], which was able to field candidates in 421 constituencies in 2022, announced that it would not attempt to field candidates with such short notice before the first round of the 2024 legislative election.<ref name="PA"/>

===Debates===
[[France 3]] and [[France Bleu]] announced they would organise more than 200 debates between local candidates which would be broadcast on local television and radio with the first set held on 19 June, followed by additional debates on 26 June and 3 July.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Lagorce|first1=Pascale|title=Législatives 2024 : les candidats de vos circonscriptions se font face ce mercredi soir, grande soirée de débats sur France 3|url=https://france3-regions.francetvinfo.fr/legislatives-2024-les-candidats-de-vos-circonscriptions-se-font-face-ce-mercredi-soir-grande-soiree-de-debats-sur-france-3-2989613.html|access-date=22 June 2024|work=France 3|date=19 June 2024|archive-date=19 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240619183417/https://france3-regions.francetvinfo.fr/legislatives-2024-les-candidats-de-vos-circonscriptions-se-font-face-ce-mercredi-soir-grande-soiree-de-debats-sur-france-3-2989613.html|url-status=live}}</ref> Between the two rounds, 23 RN candidates refused to participate or cancelled their appearances in these debates.<ref name="LMlive3"/>

[[TF1]] also announced plans to hold a debate on 25 June between [[Gabriel Attal]], [[Jordan Bardella]], and [[Manuel Bompard]].<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives: un débat télévisé Attal-Bardella-Bompard le 25 juin|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/legislatives-un-debat-televise-attal-bardella-bompard-le-25-juin_AD-202406190888.html|access-date=22 June 2024|work=BFMTV|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=19 June 2024|archive-date=22 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240622225523/https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/legislatives-un-debat-televise-attal-bardella-bompard-le-25-juin_AD-202406190888.html|url-status=live}}</ref> On 22 June, Attal, taking note of three-time presidential candidate [[Jean-Luc Mélenchon]]'s comments refusing to rule out the possibility that he might seek to become prime minister, challenged him to participate in the debate instead of Bompard, the national operations team coordinator of [[La France Insoumise]],<ref>{{cite news|last1=Quinault-Maupoil|first1=Tristan|last2=Boichot|first2=Loris|last3=Trémolet de Villers|first3=Vincent|title=Législatives: Attal demande à Mélenchon de remplacer Bompard mardi au débat télévisé|url=https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-attal-demande-a-melenchon-de-remplacer-bompard-au-debat-televise-20240623|access-date=24 June 2024|work=Le Figaro|date=23 June 2024|archive-date=25 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240625015746/https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-attal-demande-a-melenchon-de-remplacer-bompard-au-debat-televise-20240623|url-status=live}}</ref> a demand also echoed by Bardella, though Mélenchon declined.<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives 2024 : Gabriel Attal et Jordan Bardella souhaitent que Jean-Luc Mélenchon participe aux débats TV|url=https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/politique/legislatives-2024-gabriel-attal-et-jordan-bardella-souhaitent-que-jean-luc-melenchon-participe-aux-debats-tv-6928351|access-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624144904/https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/politique/legislatives-2024-gabriel-attal-et-jordan-bardella-souhaitent-que-jean-luc-melenchon-participe-aux-debats-tv-6928351|url-status=live}}</ref> [[The Republicans (France)|The Republicans]] appealed their exclusion from the TF1 debate to the ''[[Conseil d'État]]'', with the [[Regulatory Authority for Audiovisual and Digital Communication]] already having declined to take action,<ref>{{cite news|title=LR saisit le Conseil d'Etat en référé pour être invité au débat des législatives sur TF1 ce mardi|url=https://www.nicematin.com/politique/lr-saisit-le-conseil-detat-en-refere-pour-etre-invite-au-debat-des-legislatives-sur-tf1-ce-mardi-929691|access-date=24 June though this appeal was rejected the next day, a few hours before the debate.<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives : le Conseil d'État rejette la demande de participation de LR pour le débat de ce mardi soir|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-le-conseil-detat-rejette-la-demande-de-participation-de-lr-pour-le-debat-de-ce-mardi-soir-25-06-2024-BN6V3AGTRFE3NHWNAU6ERZAXUY.php|access-date=25 [[France 2]] also held a debate on 27 June between Attal, Bardella, and [[Olivier Faure]],<ref name="France2"/> during which Attal directed viewers to a calculator for retirement pensions under the [[New Popular Front]]'s plans, leading the alliance to initiate emergency proceedings against [[Renaissance (French political party)|Renaissance]] for "false and misleading allegations likely to alter the vote" under article L163-2 of the electoral code, with hearings set for 1 July.<ref>{{cite news|title=En direct, législatives 2024 : LFI saisit la justice contre Renaissance pour « diffusion de fausses informations »|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/06/28/en-direct-legislatives-2024-lfi-saisit-la-justice-contre-renaissance-pour-diffusion-de-fausses-informations_6244936_823448.html|access-date=28 June 2024|work=Le Monde|date=28 June 2024|archive-date=28 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240628143128/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/06/28/en-direct-legislatives-2024-lfi-saisit-la-justice-contre-renaissance-pour-diffusion-de-fausses-informations_6244936_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

Several debates were also initially anticipated between the two rounds, including one hosted by France 2 on 4 July. For the other two debates between the two rounds, the New Popular Front chose to send [[Marine Tondelier]] on [[BFM TV]] and [[Ian Brossat]] on [[CNews]], respecting the boycott of the channel by [[The Ecologists (political party)|The Ecologists]] and the [[Socialist Party (France)|Socialist Party]].<ref name="France2">{{cite news|title=Élections législatives : un débat Gabriel Attal, Jordan Bardella et Olivier Faure jeudi soir sur France 2|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/elections-legislatives-un-debat-gabriel-attal-jordan-bardella-et-olivier-faure-jeudi-soir-sur-france-2-24-06-2024-MV7D5MYBARHBTP7K2ZBIDGNQ2I.php|access-date=24 June 2024|work=Le Parisien|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630224732/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/elections-legislatives-un-debat-gabriel-attal-jordan-bardella-et-olivier-faure-jeudi-soir-sur-france-2-24-06-2024-MV7D5MYBARHBTP7K2ZBIDGNQ2I.php|url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives : "C'est le président de la République qui a tué la majorité présidentielle", affirme Edouard June 2024|work=Libération|date=20 June 2024|archive-date=30 June On 1 July, Bardella challenged Mélenchon to a one-on-one debate, which the latter declined, and Tondelier confirmed her participation in the third debate,<ref name="LMlive2"/> before BFM TV announced on 2 July that no debate would be held, and the three invitees would instead each be allocated a one-hour segment in a different viewing format.<ref name="LMlive3"/> Later reporting indicated that this decision was motivated by the fact that The Ecologists were allocated a smaller share of constituencies in the agreement of the [[New Popular Front]], but [[Marc-Olivier Fogiel]] publicly insisted that it was the RN's stance that forced BFM TV to call off the debate.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Condomines|first1=Anaïs|last2=Franque|first2=Adrien|title="Il n'y aura pas de débat", dit le
