l'entre-deux-tours|url=https://www.liberation.fr/checknews/debat-de-lentre-deux-tours-marine-tondelier-au-coeur-dun-imbroglio-mediatique-20240702_6IQ7JXJPKZCIHGLH432EKUOWJI/|access-date=4 July 2024|work=Libération|date=2 July 2024}}</ref> Ultimately, it was announced that none of these broadcasts would be held in a debate format.<ref name="LMlive4"/>

===Candidate incidents and controversies===

====Racism, anti-Semitism, and hate symbols====

=====Against candidates=====
[[File:2024-03-03 - Congrès du PSE- 105 - Raphael Glucksmann.jpg|thumb|upright|[[Raphaël Glucksmann]] in 2024]]
The campaign was marred by numerous incidents of [[Racism in France|racial]] and [[Antisemitism in France|anti-Semitic]] abuse. On 17 June, [[Hanane Mansouri]], [[The Republicans (France)|The Republicans]] (LR) member supported by the [[National Rally]] (RN) for [[Isère's 8th constituency]], revealed that she was inundated by [[Anti-Arab racism|anti-Arab racist abuse]] after her candidacy was confirmed.<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives : qui est Hanane Mansouri, candidate de l'alliance des droites dans l'Isère, victime d'insultes racistes ?|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-qui-est-hanane-mansouri-candidate-de-lalliance-des-droites-dans-lisere-victime-dinsultes-racistes-19-06-2024-WLSU7SSPSNC6JMYVUAEHL33DBA.php|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=19 June 2024|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630225610/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-qui-est-hanane-mansouri-candidate-de-lalliance-des-droites-dans-lisere-victime-dinsultes-racistes-19-06-2024-WLSU7SSPSNC6JMYVUAEHL33DBA.php|url-status=live}}</ref> [[La France Insoumise]] (LFI) candidate Yasmina Samri, running in [[Charente-Maritime's 1st constituency]], decided to end her candidacy after receiving numerous racist insults and threats.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Zabalza|first1=Frédéric|title=Législatives en Charente-Maritime : Yasmina Samri retire sa candidature sur la 1re circonscription|url=https://www.sudouest.fr/elections/legislatives/charente-maritime/legislatives-en-charente-maritime-yasmina-samri-retire-sa-candidature-sur-la-1re-circonscription-20214222.php|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Sud Ouest|date=21 June 2024|archive-date=21 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240621163730/https://www.sudouest.fr/elections/legislatives/charente-maritime/legislatives-en-charente-maritime-yasmina-samri-retire-sa-candidature-sur-la-1re-circonscription-20214222.php|url-status=live}}</ref> While campaigning in [[Marseille]] for the [[New Popular Front]] on 20 June, [[Raphaël Glucksmann]], accompanied by journalist [[Léa Salamé]], was recorded being told "shame on you as a Jew" by a voter after trying to give them a leaflet. He subsequently revealed that his cell phone number had been leaked on [[Telegram (software)|Telegram]] groups and he was now simultaneously being bombarded with hateful messages from members of the Jewish far-right – outraged at his involvement in the alliance – and those on the left who alleged he was a pro-[[Benjamin Netanyahu|Netanyahu]] [[Zionism|Zionist]] on the basis of his [[Ashkenazi Jews|Ashkenazic]] surname.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Rivet|first1=Solenne|title=Vidéo – Raphaël Glucksmann attaqué, il pousse un coup de gueule : "Arrêtez !"|url=https://www.gala.fr/l_actu/news_de_stars/video-raphael-glucksmann-attaque-il-pousse-un-coup-de-gueule-arretez_545935|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Gala|date=21 June 2024|archive-date=22 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240622010427/https://www.gala.fr/l_actu/news_de_stars/video-raphael-glucksmann-attaque-il-pousse-un-coup-de-gueule-arretez_545935|url-status=live}}</ref>

On 24 June, Shannon Seban, [[Renaissance (French political party)|Renaissance]] candidate for [[Val-de-Marne's 10th constituency]], announced that she filed a police complaint in response to a group of pro-[[State of Palestine|Palestine]] festivalgoers screaming "get out, dirty Zionist" at her.<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives: la candidate Renaissance Shannon Seban porte plainte pour injure raciste|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/legislatives-la-candidate-renaissance-shannon-seban-porte-plainte-pour-injure-raciste_AD-202406240320.html|access-date=24 June In [[Calvados (department)|Calvados]], the campaign posters of LFI [[Member of European Parliament|MEP]]-elect [[Emma Fourreau]] and [[Calvados's 6th constituency|6th constituency]] candidate Noé Gauchard were defaced with swastikas and neo-Nazi symbols,<ref>{{cite news|last1=Vaillant|first1=Arthus|title="Des actes abjects": des symboles nazis tagués sur des affiches du Nouveau Front populaire as were those for [[The Ecologists (France)|The Ecologists]] (LE) candidate Guillaume Hédouin in [[Manche's 1st constituency]] along with the word "Islam,"<ref>{{cite news|last1=Durand|first1=Dominique|title=Des tags racistes et antisémites sur des affiches du Nouveau Front while those for Pascaline Lécorché of [[Place Publique]] in [[Bouches-du-Rhône's 1st constituency]] were covered with "[[Hamas]] candidates" stickers.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Mothe|first1=Grégoire|title=Des bandeaux "candidates du Hamas" apposés sur des affiches du Nouveau front On the day of the first round, [[Roxane Lundy]], candidate for [[Génération.s]] in [[Oise's 1st constituency]], discovered that her campaign posters in [[Beauvais]] and [[Maignelay-Montigny]] had been defaced with swastikas.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Caffin|first1=Patrick|title=Des tags nazis sur les affiches d'une candidate du Nouveau Front populaire : " La parole raciste se libère "|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/oise-60/des-tags-nazis-sur-les-affiches-dune-candidate-du-nouveau-front-populaire-la-parole-raciste-se-libere-30-06-2024-UI5NSTU52RDVFFASARSO64HTEM.php|access-date=30 =====By candidates=====
On 17 June, ''[[Libération]]'' reported that Marie-Christine Sorin, RN candidate for [[Hautes-Pyrénées's 1st constituency]], made a tweet in January saying "No, not all civilizations are equal ... [some] have just stayed below bestiality in the evolutionary chain."<ref>{{cite news|last1=Macé|first1=Maxime|last2=Plottu|first2=Pierre|title=Législatives : le Rassemblement national et ses candidats racistes, antisémites et complotistes|url=https://www.liberation.fr/politique/legislatives-le-rassemblement-national-et-ses-candidats-racistes-antisemites-et-complotistes-20240617_SNNHEN7AGZGDZCBSUSXWVNYSZE/|access-date=25 The RN initially suspended their support for Joseph Martin, candidate for [[Morbihan's 1st constituency]], after the discovery of a 2018 tweet reading "Gas brought justice to the victims of [[the Holocaust]],"<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives 2024 : le candidat suspendu du RN pour un tweet réfute tout but reinstated him after he explained that he meant it as an allusion to the death of [[Holocaust denial|Holocaust denier]] [[Robert Faurisson]] the day prior.<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives : le RN réhabilite Joseph Martin, candidat soupçonné d'antisémitisme|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-le-rn-rehabilite-joseph-martin-candidat-soupconne-dantisemitisme-23-06-2024-G4QNGM4FIZH77CPMGBGZJL3VJ4.php|access-date=23 On 19 June, the pro-[[Éric Ciotti]] faction of LR withdrew their support for Louis-Joseph Pecher, jointly supported by the RN in [[Meurthe-et-Moselle's 5th constituency]], due to his history of "anti-Semitic, [[homophobia|homophobic]] and odious remarks."<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives 2024 : Eric Ciotti retire son soutien à un candidat accusé d'avoir publié "des messages antisémites, homophobes et orduriers"|url=https://www.francetvinfo.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-2024-eric-ciotti-retire-son-investiture-a-un-candidat-accuse-d-avoir-tenu-des-propos-antisemites_6614019.html|access-date=22 Another pro-Ciotti LR candidate supported by the RN, [[Gilles Bourdouleix]], was previously convicted for condoning [[crimes against humanity]] in 2014 for saying that "[[Adolf Hitler|Hitler]] didn't kill enough" [[Romani people]], though his sentence was suspended on the basis that he never intended for his remarks to be made public.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Guez|first1=Ariel|title=Le maire de Cholet Gilles Bourdouleix candidat aux législatives soutenu par LR et le RN|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/le-maire-de-cholet-gilles-bourdouleix-candidat-aux-legislatives-soutenu-par-lr-et-le-rn_AV-202406111034.html|access-date=26 June On 25 June, Pascal Schneider, mayor of [[Neuves-Maisons]], filed a complaint with the public prosecutor against Pierre-Nicolas Nups, candidate of the [[Party of France]] in [[Meurthe-et-Moselle's 5th constituency]], for electoral posters featuring a young white boy with blue eyes and blond hair reading "[[Fourteen Words|Let's give white children a future]]."<ref>{{cite news|last1=Braconnot|first1=Frédérique|title=" Donnons un avenir aux enfants blancs ", ce slogan qui choque sur des panneaux de Meurthe-et-Moselle|url=https://www.estrepublicain.fr/elections/2024/06/24/donnons-un-avenir-aux-enfants-blancs-le-slogan-qui-choque-dans-la-5e-circonscription|access-date=25 June 2024|work=L'Est Républicain|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=25 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240625023106/https://www.estrepublicain.fr/elections/2024/06/24/donnons-un-avenir-aux-enfants-blancs-le-slogan-qui-choque-dans-la-5e-circonscription|url-status=live}}</ref>

On 26 June, [[Reconquête]] leader [[Éric Zemmour]] shared a video of him tapping along to the rhythm of the [[TikTok]]-viral song "Je partira pas" ("I willn't [sic] leave"), which features various overtly xenophobic lyrics, with audio of the song – remixing the screams of a man being apprehended by the police while being carried off a plane in a viral video – in the background. While the song, supposedly [[Artificial intelligence art|created with AI]] by an artist under the name "Crazy-Girl," was removed for violating TikTok's content guidelines, it spread widely over social media, and was denounced by [[French Communist Party]] leader [[Fabien Roussel]].<ref>{{cite news|title=" Je partira pas " : ce que l'on sait sur cette chanson raciste que TikTok cherche à supprimer de sa plateforme|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/je-partira-pas-ce-que-lon-sait-sur-cette-chanson-raciste-que-tiktok-cherche-a-supprimer-de-sa-plateforme-27-06-2024-BI7CMQNZGVFFZO5NJ7PASMSWQQ.php|access-date=27 June 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=27 June 2024|archive-date=27 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240627140455/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/je-partira-pas-ce-que-lon-sait-sur-cette-chanson-raciste-que-tiktok-cherche-a-supprimer-de-sa-plateforme-27-06-2024-BI7CMQNZGVFFZO5NJ7PASMSWQQ.php|url-status=live}}</ref> [[SOS Racisme]] announced that it filed a complaint with the authorities regarding the song for [[Hate speech laws in France|incitement of hatred]].<ref name="JPP1">{{cite news|last1=Pezet|first1=Jacques|title=D'où vient la chanson raciste "Je partira pas" partagée par des comptes d'extrême droite ?|url=https://www.liberation.fr/checknews/dou-vient-la-chanson-raciste-je-partira-pas-partagee-par-des-comptes-dextreme-droite-20240627_B4UUUFY5YFFARHQB2AQ6GH7CKY/|access-date=27 June 2024|work=Libération|date=27 June 2024|archive-date=27 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240627133633/https://www.liberation.fr/checknews/dou-vient-la-chanson-raciste-je-partira-pas-partagee-par-des-comptes-dextreme-droite-20240627_B4UUUFY5YFFARHQB2AQ6GH7CKY/|url-status=live}}</ref> The RN also denounced the "calls for murder, violent misogyny, crude anti-Semitism and conspiracism" of the lyrics of ''No Pasarán'' which was released by a collective of rappers opposed to the far-right after the first round.<ref name="LMlive3"/>

Thierry Dussud of the RN, [[Substitute (elections)#France|substitute]] for the Ciotti-aligned LR candidate supported by the RN in [[Ardèche's 2nd constituency]], [[Vincent Trébuchet]], announced on 26 June that he would quit after racist and anti-Semitic posts he made resurfaced, including one in which he declared "Let's give the Africans back to Africa."<ref>{{cite news|last1=Berthaud|first1=Alexandre|title=Ardèche : après des propos racistes, un suppléant RN aux législatives démissionne|url=https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/politique/ardeche-apres-des-propos-raciste-s-un-suppleant-rn-aux-legislatives-demissionne-9487709|access-date=26 June 2024|work=France Bleu Drôme Ardèche|date=26 June 2024|archive-date=26 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240626142437/https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/politique/ardeche-apres-des-propos-raciste-s-un-suppleant-rn-aux-legislatives-demissionne-9487709|url-status=live}}</ref> In addition to the 20 RN candidates identified by ''Libération'' as having made racist, anti-Semitic, and discriminatory comments on social media, ''[[Mediapart]]'' also uncovered similar posts by another 24 RN candidates using their real names.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Brabant|first1=Justine|last2=Rouget|first2=Antton|title=Racisme : plus de 40 candidats RN en roue libre sur les réseaux sociaux|url=https://www.mediapart.fr/journal/france/210624/racisme-plus-de-40-candidats-rn-en-roue-libre-sur-les-reseaux-sociaux|access-date=21 June 2024|work=Mediapart|date=26 June 2024|archive-date=21 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240621215924/https://www.mediapart.fr/journal/france/210624/racisme-plus-de-40-candidats-rn-en-roue-libre-sur-les-reseaux-sociaux|url-status=live}}</ref> On 27 June, LFI withdrew its support for Reda Belkadi, candidate for [[Loir-et-Cher's 1st constituency]], after the discovery of his past anti-Semitic and homophobic tweets including anti-Jewish and anti-gay slurs.<ref name="LFPCF"/>

On 1 July, Paule Veyre de Soras, RN candidate for [[Mayenne's 1st constituency]], apologised for her comments that "my ophthalmologist is a Jew, and my dentist is a Muslim" in response to a journalist's question about racism within her party.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Cotta|first1=Martin|title=Législatives 2024 : "J'ai comme ophtalmo un juif", une candidate RN en Mayenne dérape|url=https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/politique/legislatives-2024-j-ai-comme-ophtalmo-un-juif-une-candidate-rn-en-mayenne-derape-9109662|access-date=1 July 2024|work=France Bleu Mayenne|date=1 July 2024|archive-date=1 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240701170833/https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/politique/legislatives-2024-j-ai-comme-ophtalmo-un-juif-une-candidate-rn-en-mayenne-derape-9109662|url-status=live}}</ref> On 2 July, Ludivine Daoudi, RN candidate for [[Calvados's 1st constituency]], withdrew after her NFP opponent circulated images of her wearing a Luftwaffe visor cap with a swastika on it.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Flouvat|first1=Léni|title=Info France Bleu – La candidate RN à Caen se retire après la diffusion d'une photo d'elle portant une casquette nazie|url=https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/politique/info-france-bleu-la-candidate-rn-a-caen-se-retire-apres-la-diffusion-d-une-photo-d-elle-portant-une-casquette-nazie-4821206|access-date=2 July 2024|work=France Bleu Normandie|date=2 July 2024|archive-date=6 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240706000355/https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/politique/info-france-bleu-la-candidate-rn-a-caen-se-retire-apres-la-diffusion-d-une-photo-d-elle-portant-une-casquette-nazie-4821206|url-status=live}}</ref> That same day, [[Daniel Grenon]], incumbent RN deputy for [[Yonne's 1st constituency]], was referred to the public prosecutor for saying during a debate that "North Africans came to power in 2016 ... [they] have no place in high places."<ref>{{cite news|last1=Tezkratt|first1=Julie|last2=de Souza|first2=Bradley|title=Législatives 2024 : Daniel Grenon, candidat du RN dans la 1re circonscription de l'Yonne, accusé de racisme|url=https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/politique/legislatives-2024-le-candidat-du-rn-dans-l-yonne-daniel-grenon-accuse-de-racisme-1006850|access-date=3 July 2024|work=France Bleu Auxerre|date=2 July 2024|archive-date=2 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240702174326/https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/politique/legislatives-2024-le-candidat-du-rn-dans-l-yonne-daniel-grenon-accuse-de-racisme-1006850|url-status=live}}</ref>

After regional daily ''[[La Montagne (newspaper)|La Montagne]]'' uncovered racist social media posts by Isabelle Dupré, RN candidate for [[Puy-de-Dôme's 2nd constituency]], she responded "If I'm elected, I'll stop the racist humor." Reporting also uncovered photos in which Julie Apricena, substitute to Pierre Gentillet, RN candidate for [[Cher's 3rd constituency]], was accompanied by neo-Nazi skinheads and wearing a T-shirt reading "White Pride, World Wide."<ref name="LMlive3"/> On 3 July, Jean-Yves Le Boulanger, RN candidate for [[Côtes-d'Armor's 5th constituency]], denied that he was a "fascist" because [[I'm not racist, I have black friends|he has "friends of colour"]] and didn't use his motorcycle to run over "a coloured priest who blessed" him.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Schweitzer|first1=Baptiste|title=Côtes-d'Armor : un candidat RN se défend d'être "facho" car il n'a pas "écrasé le curé de couleur" avec sa moto|url=https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/elections/cotes-d-armor-un-candidat-rn-se-defend-d-etre-facho-car-il-n-a-pas-ecrase-le-cure-de-couleur-avec-sa-moto-3520275|access-date=3 July 2024|work=France Bleu Breizh Izel|date=3 July 2024|archive-date=6 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240706000353/https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/elections/cotes-d-armor-un-candidat-rn-se-defend-d-etre-facho-car-il-n-a-pas-ecrase-le-cure-de-couleur-avec-sa-moto-3520275|url-status=live}}</ref> The same day, Laurent Gnaedig, RN candidate for [[Haut-Rhin's 1st constituency]], said that he believed [[Jean-Marie Le Pen]]'s comments that gas chambers were a mere "detail" of World War II were not anti-Semitic, and added that he had "doubts" about Le Pen's conviction for dismissing crimes against humanity.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Lalemant|first1=Alexis|title=Législatives: pour le RN Laurent Gnaedig, les propos de Jean-Marie Le Pen sur les chambres à gaz "n'étaient pas une remarque antisémite"|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/alsace/legislatives-pour-le-rn-laurent-gnaedig-les-propos-de-jean-marie-le-pen-sur-les-chambres-a-gaz-n-etaient-pas-une-remarque-antisemite_AV-202407030890.html|access-date=3 A civil servant of Moroccan origin accused Philippe Torre, RN candidate for [[Aisne's 2nd constituency]], of making racist statements in an altercation on 3 July by implying that he would be deported despite being a French national.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Sulzer|first1=Alexandre|title=Législatives : un candidat LR-RN accusé d'agression verbale raciste par un employé ====Physical attacks involving candidates and activists====
Several candidates also reported attacks against them and activists supporting them over the course of the campaign. [[Florian Chauche]], LFI candidate and incumbent deputy for [[Territoire de Belfort's 2nd constituency]], decried physical attacks and the usage of racist slurs against his supporters on 17 June.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Cornuez|first1=Benjamin|title=Des militants LFI victimes d'insultes racistes à Belfort pendant leur campagne|url=https://www.estrepublicain.fr/faits-divers-justice/2024/06/18/des-militants-lfi-victimes-d-insultes-racistes-pendant-leur-campagne|access-date=22 June 2024|work=L'Est Républicain|date=18 On 20 June, Hervé Breuil, RN candidate for [[Loire's 2nd constituency]], alleged that a group of masked individuals struck him from behind and pelted him with rotten fruit while hurling verbal abuse at him.<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives : un candidat RN "chahuté" et "agressé verbalement" à Saint-Étienne, une enquête ouverte|url=https://www.tf1info.fr/elections/video-elections-legislatives-saint-etienne-un-candidat-rn-rassemblement-national-chahute-et-agresse-verbalement-dans-la-loire-une-enquete-ouverte-2305074.html|access-date=22 On 23 June, numerous left-wing activists (for LE candidate Céline Papin in [[Gironde's 1st constituency]], LE candidate and outgoing deputy [[Sabrina Sebaihi]] in [[Hauts-de-Seine's 4th constituency]], and [[Socialist Party (France)|Socialist Party]] (PS) candidate Joao Martins Pereira in [[Val-de-Marne's 8th constituency]]) reported being assaulted and threatened by supporters of the far-right.<ref name="NM22">{{cite news|title=Législatives: plusieurs agressions de militants de gauche qui dénoncent l'extrême droite|url=https://www.nicematin.com/faits-divers/legislatives-plusieurs-agressions-de-militants-de-gauche-qui-denoncent-lextreme-droite-929381|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Nice-Matin|agency=Agence Séverine Vézies, LFI candidate for [[Doubs's 1st constituency]], claimed that a self-proclaimed RN supporter attempted to strike a man in his 80s with a broomstick while putting up a campaign poster for her on 25 June.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Deshayes|first1=Emmanuel|title="Ces gens n'aiment pas la démocratie" : une plainte déposée après l'agression d'un militant du Nouveau Front Populaire à [[Danielle Simonnet]], LFI deputy for [[Paris's 15th constituency]], organised a "rally against the far-right" after four of her supporters were tear-gassed, assaulted, and called "anti-Semitic bastards" by a group of far-right supporters while putting up election posters in the [[20th arrondissement of Paris]] on the evening of 2 July.<ref>{{cite news|last1=De On 3 July, RN MEP [[Marie Dauchy]], candidate for [[Savoie's 3rd constituency]], announced she was suspending campaigning after being attacked at the market in [[La Rochette, Savoie|La Rochette]], with a merchant allegedly trying to kick her while tearing up her campaign leaflets.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Gallotti|first1=Anabelle|title=Législatives 2024 : Marie Dauchy, candidate RN en Savoie dit On the evening of 3 July, [[Prisca Thevenot]], [[Spokesperson of the Government of France]] and Renaissance candidate for [[Hauts-de-Seine's 8th constituency]], along with her substitute {{ill|Virginie Lanlo|fr}} and one of her supporters, were attacked by a group of fifteen people while putting up campaign posters in [[Meudon]], with four of them arrested following the attack. The supporter in question was struck in the face using a scooter, breaking their jaw, while Lanlo was punched and kicked, while Thevenot herself escaped uninjured.<ref name="Thevenot">{{cite news|last1=Fournier|first1=Catherine|title=Législatives 2024 : ce que l'on sait de l'agression de la porte-parole du gouvernement Prisca Thevenot lors d'un collage d'affiches à Meudon|url=https://www.francetvinfo.fr/elections/legislatives/elections-legislatives-2024-ce-que-l-on-sait-de-l-agression-de-la-porte-parole-du-gouvernement-prisca-thevenot-lors-d-un-collage-d-affiches-a-meudon_6645543.html|access-date=4 July 2024|work=franceinfo|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=4 July 2024|archive-date=4 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240704162235/https://www.francetvinfo.fr/elections/legislatives/elections-legislatives-2024-ce-que-l-on-sait-de-l-agression-de-la-porte-parole-du-gouvernement-prisca-thevenot-lors-d-un-collage-d-affiches-a-meudon_6645543.html|url-status=live}}</ref> Bernard Dupré, deputy mayor of [[La Tronche]], was punched in the right eye by a man who he says claimed to be an LFI supporter on 4 July while putting up campaign posters for the campaign of [[Olivier Véran]], Renaissance candidate for [[Isère's 1st constituency]],<ref>{{cite news|last1=Pueyo|first1=Véronique|title=Législatives 2024 : en Isère, un élu agressé alors qu'il collait des affiches pour Olivier Véran|url=https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/faits-divers-justice/isere-agresse-alors-qu-il-collait-des-affiches-pour-olivier-veran-5362320|access-date=4 July 2024|work=France Bleu Isère|date=4 July 2024|archive-date=6 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240706000906/https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/faits-divers-justice/isere-agresse-alors-qu-il-collait-des-affiches-pour-olivier-veran-5362320|url-status=live}}</ref> though the attacker claimed that Dupré was the first one to strike him.<ref name="LMlive5"/>

On 4 July, [[Thomas Mesnier]], former [[Horizons (political party)|Horizons]] deputy and candidate for [[Charente's 1st constituency]], reported that one of his supporters had been kicked, punched, and targeted by homophobic insults by a group of four people while putting up posters in [[Angoulême]].<ref>{{cite news|last1=Marsat|first1=Pierre|title=Législatives 2024 : un proche de Thomas Mesnier That evening, [[Geoffroy Didier]], LR candidate for [[Hauts-de-Seine's 6th constituency]], reported that one of his supporters had been "violently assaulted and threatened with death" in [[Neuilly-sur-Seine]] while leafleting for his campaign.<ref>{{cite news|title=EN DIRECT – Législatives : "Il y a encore la capacité d'avoir la majorité absolue ", estime Marine Le Three supporters of Maxime Viancin, LFI candidate for [[Loire-Atlantique's 10th constituency]], were chased down the street by an RN supporter who screamed "Bardella will take care of the lefties, dykes and trans" at them before pushing one and punching another, while his wife joined him on the street while waving a French flag.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Bonhoure|first1=Matthieu|title=Législatives On 2 July, ''Le Courrier de la Mayenne'' resurfaced a report from 12 January 1995 about Annie-Claire Jaccoud Bell, RN candidate for [[Mayenne's 3rd constituency]], engaging in an attempted armed hostage-taking at the [[Ernée]] town hall, firing a single wayward shot from a rifle she smuggled into the town hall while fighting with a secretary.<ref>{{cite news|title=Mayenne. Les casseroles d'Annie Bell, candidate du RN en Mayenne : elle avait commis une prise d'otage armée en 1995|url=https://www.lecourrierdelamayenne.fr/actualite-25752-mayenne-les-casseroles-d-annie-bell-candidate-du-rn-en-mayenne-elle-avait-commis-une-prise-d-otage-armee-en-1995|access-date=2 July 2024|work=Le Courrier de la Mayenne|date=2 July 2024|archive-date=2 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240702200335/https://www.lecourrierdelamayenne.fr/actualite-25752-mayenne-les-casseroles-d-annie-bell-candidate-du-rn-en-mayenne-elle-avait-commis-une-prise-d-otage-armee-en-1995|url-status=live}}</ref>

In anticipation of potential violence after the second round, [[Minister of the Interior (France)|Minister of the Interior]] [[Gérald Darmanin]] announced that 30,000 police would be deployed across the country on the evening of 7 July.<ref name="Thevenot"/> He also announced on the morning of 5 July that despite the short campaign, 51 different candidates, substitutes, and supporters had been physically attacked, often suffering significant injuries requiring medical attention in the process, with more than 30 arrests having been made among people with "extremely varied profiles."<ref name="LMlive5">{{cite news|title=En direct, législatives 2024 : posez vos questions sur la campagne de l'entre-deux-tours à la cheffe du service politique du « Monde »|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/05/en-direct-legislatives-2024-voter-pour-un-candidat-de-la-france-insoumise-n-est-plus-un-vote-de-c-ur-mais-un-vote-de-raison-pour-eviter-la-catastrophe-estime-raphael-glucksmann_6245747_823448.html|access-date=5 July 2024|work=Le Monde|date=5 July 2024|archive-date=5 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240705063659/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/05/en-direct-legislatives-2024-voter-pour-un-candidat-de-la-france-insoumise-n-est-plus-un-vote-de-c-ur-mais-un-vote-de-raison-pour-eviter-la-catastrophe-estime-raphael-glucksmann_6245747_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

====Death threats====
Many candidates also reported receiving [[death threat]]s both online and in real life. On 15 June, [[Jean-Jacques Gaultier]], LR candidate for [[Vosges's 4th constituency]], reported receiving a death threat via post.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Barraux|first1=Tristan|title=Législatives 2024 : "tu dois renoncer", le candidat vosgien Jean-Jacques Gaultier menacé de mort par courrier|url=https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/faits-divers-justice/legislatives-2024-le-candidat-vosgien-jean-jacques-gautier-menace-de-mort-par-courrier-7173860|access-date=22 June 2024|work=France Bleu|date=16 June 2024|archive-date=17 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240617150819/https://www.francebleu.fr/infos/faits-divers-justice/legislatives-2024-le-candidat-vosgien-jean-jacques-gautier-menace-de-mort-par-courrier-7173860|url-status=live}}</ref> On 19 June, Elsa Richard, LE candidate for [[Maine-et-Loire's 1st constituency]], reported messages from people threatening to behead her in front of her house to the police.<ref>{{cite news|title=Une candidate du Nouveau Front populaire aux législatives porte plainte pour menaces de mort|url=https://www.ouest-france.fr/elections/legislatives/une-candidate-du-nouveau-front-populaire-aux-legislatives-porte-plainte-pour-menaces-de-mort-66cdce6e-2ed8-11ef-9d8b-818edcab8630|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Ouest-France|date=20 June 2024|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630212032/https://www.ouest-france.fr/elections/legislatives/une-candidate-du-nouveau-front-populaire-aux-legislatives-porte-plainte-pour-menaces-de-mort-66cdce6e-2ed8-11ef-9d8b-818edcab8630|url-status=live}}</ref> On 21 June, [[Pierre Morel-À-L'Huissier]], [[miscellaneous centre]] candidate and outgoing deputy for [[Lozère's constituency]], filed a police complaint after discovering a large tag with a death threat against him in [[Gorges du Tarn Causses]].<ref>{{cite news|last1=Guignard|first1=Célian|title=Législatives en Lozère : "Mort À L'Huissier", un tag odieux découvert à Blajoux à l'encontre du député sortant|url=https://www.midilibre.fr/2024/06/21/legislatives-en-lozere-mort-a-lhuissier-un-tag-odieux-decouvert-a-blajoux-a-lencontre-du-depute-sortant-12032146.php|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Midi Libre|date=21 June 2024|archive-date=22 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240622015253/https://www.midilibre.fr/2024/06/21/legislatives-en-lozere-mort-a-lhuissier-un-tag-odieux-decouvert-a-blajoux-a-lencontre-du-depute-sortant-12032146.php|url-status=live}}</ref><ref name="LM1"/> After being targeted by extensive harassment and numerous death threats on social media, Ethan Leys, RN candidate for [[Nord's 8th constituency]], filed a police complaint and suspended in-person campaign activities.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Monforta|first1=Marion|title=Législatives : le candidat RN Ethan Leys porte plainte pour harcèlement et menaces de mort|url=https://www.lejdd.fr/politique/legislatives-le-candidat-rn-ethan-leys-porte-plainte-pour-harcelement-et-menaces-de-mort-146505|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Le Journal du Dimanche|date=18 June 2024|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630224734/https://www.lejdd.fr/politique/legislatives-le-candidat-rn-ethan-leys-porte-plainte-pour-harcelement-et-menaces-de-mort-146505|url-status=live}}</ref> While attending a [[France 3]] Franche-Comté debate, a supporter of Philippe Ghiles, Reconquête candidate for [[Haute-Saône's 1st constituency]], threatened to kill the debate host, prompting the latter to file a complaint with the police.<ref>{{cite news|title=" Je vais le buter " : menacé lors d'un débat télévisé, un journaliste de France 3 porte plainte|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/je-vais-le-buter-menace-lors-dun-debat-televise-un-journaliste-de-france-3-porte-plainte-28-06-2024-PPBNEW4DTRBYXF2JEBNVJISWXQ.php|access-date=28 June 2024|work=Le Parisien|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=28 June 2024|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630224734/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/je-vais-le-buter-menace-lors-dun-debat-televise-un-journaliste-de-france-3-porte-plainte-28-06-2024-PPBNEW4DTRBYXF2JEBNVJISWXQ.php|url-status=live}}</ref> [[Babette de Rozières]], candidate jointly supported by Ciotti and the RN in [[Yvelines's 7th constituency]], asserted that she was targeted with death threats and racist comments after her candidacy was unveiled.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Lecoeuvre|first1=Sarah|title="Ça n'a rien à voir avec le Front national" : investie par le Rassemblement national, Babette de Rozières défend Jordan Bardella|url=https://tvmag.lefigaro.fr/programme-tv/people/ca-n-a-rien-a-voir-avec-le-front-national-investie-par-le-rassemblement-national-babette-de-rozieres-defend-jordan-bardella-20240703|access-date=4 July 2024|work=Le Figaro|date=3 July 2024|archive-date=3 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240703135437/https://tvmag.lefigaro.fr/programme-tv/people/ca-n-a-rien-a-voir-avec-le-front-national-investie-par-le-rassemblement-national-babette-de-rozieres-defend-jordan-bardella-20240703|url-status=live}}</ref> After a hundred lawyers signed on to an anti-RN letter in ''[[Marianne (magazine)|Marianne]]'', the far-right website ''Réseau libre'' published an article calling for the murder of all of its signatories.<ref name="LMlive4">{{cite news|title=En direct, législatives 2024 : agressions de militants, propos racistes, menaces contre des avocats... La campagne se tend à trois jours du second tour|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/04/en-direct-legislatives-2024-la-porte-parole-du-gouvernement-prisca-thevenot-prise-a-partie-en-tractant-a-meudon-une-enquete-ouverte_6245747_823448.html|access-date=4 July 2024|work=Le Monde|date=4 July 2024|archive-date=4 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240704071116/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/04/en-direct-legislatives-2024-la-porte-parole-du-gouvernement-prisca-thevenot-prise-a-partie-en-tractant-a-meudon-une-enquete-ouverte_6245747_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

In addition, Alice Cordier, head of the [[Feminism|feminist]] and [[Identitarian movement|white identitarian]] group [[Collectif Némésis]], filed a complaint for death threats recorded on 16 October 2023 made against her by [[Raphaël Arnault]], LFI candidate in [[Vaucluse's 1st constituency]] and a spokesperson for the [[Jeune Garde Antifasciste]] with several "[[fiche S|S cards]]" (which have often been applied to individuals considered potential threats to [[national security]]) to his name.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Eustache|first1=Thomas|title="Une balle dans la tête" : le Collectif Némésis diffuse l'enregistrement des menaces de Raphaël Arnault contre Alice Cordier|url=https://www.lejdd.fr/politique/une-balle-dans-la-tete-le-collectif-nemesis-diffuse-lenregistrement-des-menaces-de-raphael-arnault-contre-alice-cordier-146603|access-date=22 June 2024|work=Le Journal du Dimanche|date=20 June 2024|archive-date=22 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240622115437/https://www.lejdd.fr/politique/une-balle-dans-la-tete-le-collectif-nemesis-diffuse-lenregistrement-des-menaces-de-raphael-arnault-contre-alice-cordier-146603|url-status=live}}</ref>

==Results==

===National results===
Results listed below correspond to the groupings created by the [[Minister of the Interior (France)|Ministry of the Interior]], which may differ slightly from the figures reported in other sources due to reclassification of candidates into different political parties and alliances. Differences noted in the footnotes of the national results table below reflect political parties and alliances attributed to candidates by ''[[Le Monde]]''. The Ministry of the Interior classifications generally include fewer candidates within the groupings for [[Together (coalition)|Ensemble]], the [[New Popular Front]], and [[The Republicans (France)|The Republicans]] when compared with ''Le Monde'' and other media outlets which opt to not use the Ministry of the Interior's candidate classifications; as a result, the official vote and seat totals listed below may be lower than the ones reported in those sources.<ref name="LM1"/><ref name="results2024"/>

On the basis of the final results published by the Ministry of the Interior and candidate classifications of ''Le Monde'', the New Popular Front obtained 182 seats, compared to Ensemble with 168, RN-supported candidates with 143, and 45 for LR (compared with 56 claimed by the party, due to differences in candidate self-identification). Out of those 182 NFP deputies, 74 are attributed to LFI, 59 to the PS, 28 to LE, 9 to the PCF, 5 to Génération.s, 5 to miscellaneous left deputies, and 2 to regionalists. ''Le Monde'' also tallied 102 Renaissance, 33 MoDem, 26 Horizons, 3 miscellaneous centre, and 2 UDI deputies, as well as 1 deputy each under the labels of miscellaneous right and [[Agir (France)|Agir]]. The Ministry of the Interior does not classify candidates by party but rather by "political nuances" as defined within the {{ill|National Directory of Elected Officials|fr|Répertoire national des élus}}, so no official breakdown of the results of NFP or Ensemble candidates by self-declared party is available.<ref name="LMlive6"/><ref name="LM1"/><ref name="results2024"/> Although nuances for several components of those alliances were provided in 2024, neither are fully compatibilised with the actual or self-declared affiliation of candidates within these alliances.{{efn|name="NFPtotal"}}{{efn|name="Etotal"}}

===First round===
{{Bar box
|float=right
|title=Second round configurations<br/>(before candidate withdrawals)<ref name="quadrangulaires"/>
|left1=Parties (including allies,<br/>as classified by franceinfo)
|bars=
{{bar pixel|Four-way runoffs|purple|1.25||5}}
{{bar pixel|NFP–ENS–RN|blue|62.5||250}}
{{bar pixel|NFP–LR–RN|blue|10.75||43}}
{{bar pixel|Other three-way runoffs|blue|4||16}}
{{bar pixel|NFP–RN|green|16.75||67}}
{{bar pixel|RN–ENS|green|8||32}}
{{bar pixel|LR–RN|green|7||28}}
{{bar pixel|NFP–ENS|green|6.75||27}}
{{bar pixel|LR–NFP|green|1.25||5}}
{{bar pixel|LR–ENS|green|0.5||2}}
{{bar pixel|Other duels|green|7.25||29}}
{{bar pixel|Directly elected|orange|19||76}}
}}
Turnout in the first round of the legislative elections was exceptionally high, including 2.7 million [[proxy voting]] requests, with pollsters estimating the final turnout to be the highest for the first round of a legislative election since [[1997 French legislative election|1997]],<ref name="Ipsos1997">{{cite news|title=Du jamais-vu depuis 46 ans à 17h : vers un taux de participation record pour les législatives ?|url=https://www.francetvinfo.fr/elections/legislatives/du-jamais-vu-depuis-43-ans-vers-un-taux-de-participation-record-pour-les-legislatives_6635610.html|access-date=30 June 2024|work=franceinfo|date=30 June 2024|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630125610/https://www.francetvinfo.fr/elections/legislatives/du-jamais-vu-depuis-43-ans-vers-un-taux-de-participation-record-pour-les-legislatives_6635610.html|url-status=live}}</ref> which was confirmed in the provisional results with turnout at 66.71%. In the first round, the RN and their allies secured the largest share of the vote in the first round with 33.21%<!-- PLEASE DO NOT CHANGE in accordance with non-official sources: calculated according to the official figures of the Ministry of the Interior, NOT according to the unofficial candidate classifications created by various other media outlets --> of the vote, followed by the parties of the New Popular Front with 28.21%<!-- PLEASE DO NOT CHANGE, see footnote B: calculated according to the official figures of the Ministry of the Interior, NOT according to the unofficial candidate classifications created by various other media outlets -->,{{efn|name="NFPtotal"}} those of Ensemble with 21.28%<!-- PLEASE DO NOT CHANGE, see footnote C: calculated according to the official figures of the Ministry of the Interior, NOT according to the unofficial candidate classifications created by various other media outlets -->,{{efn|name="Etotal"}} and LR candidates with 6.57%<!-- PLEASE DO NOT CHANGE in accordance with non-official sources: calculated according to the official figures of the Ministry of the Interior, NOT according to the unofficial candidate classifications created by various other media outlets -->, with an overall turnout of 66.71%.<ref name="results2024"/>

On the basis of the first round results (not accounting for candidate withdrawals after the first round), 306 constituencies were headed to three-way runoffs and 5 to four-way runoffs,<ref name="quadrangulaires"/> with only 89 three-way and 2 four-way runoffs remaining after candidate withdrawals announced ahead of the registration deadline for the second round.<ref name="LMwithdrawals"/> A total of 76 candidates were directly elected in the first round,<ref name="results2024"/> and RN-supported candidates qualified for the second round in 444 other constituencies, compared to 415 for the NFP, 321 for Ensemble, and 63 for LR (according to ''[[Le Monde]]'''s classifications of candidates by political affiliation).<ref name="LMresults">{{cite news|last1=Aubert|first1=Raphaëlle|last2=Sanchez|first2=Léa|last3=Breteau|first3=Pierre|last4=Romain|first4=Manon|last5=Ferrer|first5=Maxime|title=La carte des résultats des législatives au premier tour et le tableau des candidats qualifiés|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/les-decodeurs/article/2024/06/30/la-carte-des-resultats-des-legislatives-au-premier-tour-et-le-tableau-des-candidats-qualifies_6245574_4355771.html|access-date=30 June 2024|work=Le Monde|date=30 June 2024|language=fr|archive-date=1 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240701030827/https://www.lemonde.fr/les-decodeurs/article/2024/07/01/la-carte-des-resultats-des-legislatives-au-premier-tour-et-le-tableau-des-candidats-qualifies_6245574_4355771.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

===Voting instructions and withdrawals===

====Before the first round====
In an interview with [[Cyril Hanouna]] on [[Europe 1]] on 24 June, [[Minister for Gender Equality, Diversity and Equal Opportunities|Gender Equality Minister]] [[Aurore Bergé]], like [[Emmanuel Macron]], declined to specify second-round voting instructions between either the [[New Popular Front]] (NFP) and [[National Rally]] (RN) while also implying that any such discussions would not take place until after the first round.<ref>{{cite news|title=Cyril Hanouna – "Le meilleur rempart contre le Front Populaire c'est nous !", affirme Aurore Bergé|url=https://www.europe1.fr/emissions/on-marche-sur-la-tete/cyril-hanouna-le-meilleur-rempart-contre-le-front-populaire-cest-nous-declare-aurore-berge-4254521|access-date=25 June 2024|work=Europe 1|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=25 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240625020735/https://www.europe1.fr/emissions/on-marche-sur-la-tete/cyril-hanouna-le-meilleur-rempart-contre-le-front-populaire-cest-nous-declare-aurore-berge-4254521|url-status=live}}</ref><ref name="Berge"/> Both of [[Renaissance (French political party)|Renaissance]]'s alliance partners' leaders, [[François Bayrou]] of the [[Democratic Movement (France)|Democratic Movement]] (MoDem) and [[Édouard Philippe]] of [[Horizons (political party)|Horizons]], also refused to address the issue, with allies of Macron reportedly divided on this question.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Herbemont|first1=Aurélie|title=Législatives 2024 : le camp présidentiel s'interroge sur la position à tenir en cas de duel RN – Nouveau Front populaire|url=https://www.francetvinfo.fr/replay-radio/le-brief-politique/legislatives-2024-le-camp-presidentiel-s-interroge-sur-la-position-a-tenir-en-cas-de-duel-rn-nouveau-front-populaire_6587058.html|access-date=25 June 2024|work=franceinfo|date=20 June 2024|archive-date=25 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240625024403/https://www.francetvinfo.fr/replay-radio/le-brief-politique/legislatives-2024-le-camp-presidentiel-s-interroge-sur-la-position-a-tenir-en-cas-de-duel-rn-nouveau-front-populaire_6587058.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

On the afternoon of 25 June, Macron and the leaders of Renaissance, MoDem, Horizons, the [[Union of Democrats and Independents]] (UDI), the [[Radical Party (France)|Radical Party]], and several other members of his coterie met to discuss the matter, with a general consensus emerging among participants to call to block the RN and [[La France Insoumise]] (LFI) candidates in the second round and potentially withdraw on a case-by-case basis, though no decision was reached by the end of the meeting.<ref name="LP0625">{{cite news|last1=Théveniaud|first1=Pauline|title=Législatives : après une réunion avec Macron, le camp présidentiel vers un " ni RN, ni LFI " au second tour|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-apres-une-reunion-avec-macron-le-camp-presidentiel-vers-un-ni-rn-ni-lfi-au-second-tour-25-06-2024-URNVFUPA25DHTCHF5QJAAEO5PA.php|access-date=25 June 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=25 June 2024|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630224736/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-apres-une-reunion-avec-macron-le-camp-presidentiel-vers-un-ni-rn-ni-lfi-au-second-tour-25-06-2024-URNVFUPA25DHTCHF5QJAAEO5PA.php|url-status=live}}</ref> Interviewed on the evening of 26 June, Bayrou remarked, "we will vote for neither a National Rally nor LFI candidate ... why have the political forces, which I consider to be republicans, gone and settled themselves under the yoke of a very radical, brutal, violent far-left?"<ref name="Pradie"/> Philippe then called on all third-placed Horizons candidates who advanced to give up their candidacy in the second round.<ref name="LMlive"/>

[[Marine Tondelier]], leader of [[The Ecologists (political party)|The Ecologists]], announced in an interview the same day that candidates from her party would withdraw if they were eligible to advance to the second round but finished in third place,<ref>{{cite news|last1=Lecach|first1=Marianne|title=Législatives : les candidats écologistes prêts à se désister au second tour pour faire échouer le RN|url=https://www.lejdd.fr/politique/legislatives-les-candidats-ecologistes-prets-se-desister-au-second-tour-pour-faire-echouer-le-rn-146763|access-date=25 June 2024|work=Le Journal du Dimanche|date=24 June 2024|archive-date=24 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240624223750/https://www.lejdd.fr/politique/legislatives-les-candidats-ecologistes-prets-se-desister-au-second-tour-pour-faire-echouer-le-rn-146763|url-status=live}}</ref> a view also shared by [[Raphaël Glucksmann]] of [[Place Publique]].<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives : en cas de triangulaire, le moins bien placé face au RN devra se retirer, selon Glucksmann|url=https://www.challenges.fr/politique/legislatives-en-cas-de-triangulaire-le-moins-bien-place-face-au-rn-devra-se-retirer-selon-glucksmann_897177|access-date=25 June 2024|work=Challenges|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=21 June 2024|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630212555/https://www.challenges.fr/politique/legislatives-en-cas-de-triangulaire-le-moins-bien-place-face-au-rn-devra-se-retirer-selon-glucksmann_897177|url-status=live}}</ref> LFI [[Member of European Parliament|MEP]] [[Manon Aubry]] stated that the decisions of LFI candidates in three-way races would be made on a case-by-case basis.<ref>{{cite news|title=En direct, législatives 2024 : « Rien ne me choque », déclare Eric Ciotti à propos du programme du Rassemblement national|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/06/25/en-direct-legislatives-2024-suivez-la-campagne-et-les-reactions-avant-le-premier-debat-televise_6243506_823448.html|access-date=25 June 2024|work=Le Monde|date=25 June 2024|archive-date=25 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240625052451/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/06/25/en-direct-legislatives-2024-suivez-la-campagne-et-les-reactions-avant-le-premier-debat-televise_6243506_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref> [[Socialist Party (France)|Socialist Party]] leader [[Olivier Faure]], along with Glucksmann, Tondelier, and two government ministers ([[Clément Beaune]] and [[Agnès Pannier-Runacher]]) signed onto an open letter published in ''[[Le Monde]]'' on 25 June pushing for all parties facing to reach an agreement to withdraw candidates in order to block the RN, though no LFI representatives signed onto the letter.<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives 2024 : plus de 220 personnalités réclament un accord de désistement face au RN|url=https://www.ouest-france.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-2024-plus-de-220-personnalites-reclament-un-accord-de-desistement-face-au-rn-9b455068-32c5-11ef-8462-4d5d263c07bc|access-date=25 June 2024|work=Ouest-France|date=25 June 2024|archive-date=25 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240625081602/https://www.ouest-france.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-2024-plus-de-220-personnalites-reclament-un-accord-de-desistement-face-au-rn-9b455068-32c5-11ef-8462-4d5d263c07bc|url-status=live}}</ref> On 26 June, [[Jean-Luc Mélenchon]] indicated that LFI would issue voting instructions after the first round and told his supporters to not vote for the RN.<ref name="LPFaure"/> In a press release on 27 June, the [[French Communist Party]] (PCF) confirmed that it would instruct its voters to support a "republican candidate" against the RN in the second round, and that its candidates would withdraw if they advanced to the second round but finished third in the first.<ref name="LFPCF">{{cite news|title=EN DIRECT – Législatives 2024 : le RN a établi une liste de 50 postes interdits aux binationaux|url=https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/en-direct-legislatives-2024-une-majorite-de-francais-redoute-des-manifestations-violentes-20240627|access-date=27 June 2024|work=Le Figaro|date=27 June 2024|archive-date=27 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240627112924/https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/en-direct-legislatives-2024-une-majorite-de-francais-redoute-des-manifestations-violentes-20240627|url-status=live}}</ref>

While he was opposed to the prospect of an alliance between [[The Republicans (France)|The Republicans]] (LR) and the National Rally, LR vice president [[François-Xavier Bellamy]] declared that he would support candidates of the RN against those of the NFP in the second round, even in the case that they were not LFI candidates.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Sdiri|first1=Noah|title=Législatives : Bellamy voterait "bien sûr" pour le RN face à la gauche au second tour|url=https://www.lejdd.fr/politique/legislatives-bellamy-voterait-bien-sur-pour-le-rn-face-la-gauche-au-second-tour-146338|access-date=25 June 2024|work=Le Journal du Dimanche|date=13 June 2024|archive-date=27 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240627013438/https://www.lejdd.fr/politique/legislatives-bellamy-voterait-bien-sur-pour-le-rn-face-la-gauche-au-second-tour-146338|url-status=live}}</ref> In an interview on 26 June, [[Julien Aubert]] declared that he would vote for any candidate against the RN in most cases, but would vote for them if faced with a LFI candidate.<ref name="Pradie">{{cite news|title=EN DIRECT – Législatives 2024 : la France plongée dans une crise «sans précédent», s'alarme le Cese|url=https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/en-direct-legislatives-2024-a-j-4-du-premier-tour-aurelien-pradie-quitte-les-republicains-20240626|access-date=26 June 2024|work=Le Figaro|date=26 June 2024|archive-date=26 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240626063200/https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/en-direct-legislatives-2024-a-j-4-du-premier-tour-aurelien-pradie-quitte-les-republicains-20240626|url-status=live}}</ref>

====After the first round====
{{Bar box
|float=right
|title=Second round withdrawals by configuration of qualified candidates<ref name="results2024"/><ref name="LMwithdrawals"/>
|left1=Parties (including allies, as classified by ''Le Monde'')

{{bar pixel|NFP–ENS–RN, NFP withdrawal|#{{HexShade|{{party color|New Popular Front}}|0.8}}|99}}

{{bar pixel|Other three-way races with one withdrawal|#{{HexShade|{{party color|Miscellaneous}}|0.8}}|14}}
}}
In a press release after the first round, Ensemble announced that they would call upon third-placed candidates to withdraw in constituencies where other candidates "with shared values" were able to beat the RN, including the possibility of desisting in favour of selected LFI candidates.<ref name="LMlive"/> Bergé, interviewed after the first round, reaffirmed that candidates would withdraw to block the RN except in the case that it might help to elect an LFI deputy, with other parties in the alliance sharing a similar line of case-by-case withdrawals in runoffs with LFI candidates,<ref name="LMlive2"/> but Attal also emphasised that withdrawals did not constitute endorsements and that the alliance would not officially issue any voting instructions, even if individual candidates did.<ref name="LMlive3"/>

A story published by ''[[Le Monde]]'' on 5 July suggested that Attal spearheaded the anti-RN blockade to Macron's chagrin, with the latter annoyed by Attal's relative independence. Macron also called Ensemble candidates to pressure them to not drop out up until the last moment, with his inner circle reportedly becoming more comfortable with the idea of an RN victory even as Attal warned about the dangers of the far-right coming to power.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Gatinois|first1=Claire|last2=Segaunes|first2=Nathalie|last3=Trippenbach|first3=Ivanne|title=Législatives 2024 : entre l'Elysée et Matignon, tensions sur le front républicain|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/07/05/legislatives-2024-entre-l-elysee-et-matignon-tensions-sur-le-front-republicain_6247185_823448.html|access-date=5 July 2024|work=Le Monde|date=5 July 2024|archive-date=6 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240706000911/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/07/05/legislatives-2024-entre-l-elysee-et-matignon-tensions-sur-le-front-republicain_6247185_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

Mélenchon ultimately announced that all third-placed candidates of the New Popular Front who advanced to the second round in constituencies where the RN placed first would stand down.<ref name="LMlive">{{cite news|title=En direct, résultats législatives 2024 : le RN et ses alliés (34 %) devancent la coalition de gauche du NFP (28,1 %) et le camp présidentiel (20,3 %)|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/06/30/en-direct-resultats-legislatives-2024-paroles-d-electeurs-c-est-tellement-important-cette-fois_6245488_823448.html|access-date=30 June 2024|work=Le Monde|date=30 June 2024|archive-date=30 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240630183832/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/06/30/en-direct-resultats-legislatives-2024-paroles-d-electeurs-c-est-tellement-important-cette-fois_6245488_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref> In duels between left-of-centre candidates, the PS called for voters to support the higher-placed candidate, as well as for the withdrawal of lower-placed candidates,<ref name="LMlive3">{{cite news|title=En direct, législatives 2024 : plusieurs figures du camp présidentiel se désistent, à deux heures de la fin du dépôt des candidatures pour le second tour|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/02/en-direct-legislatives-2024-suivez-la-campagne-du-second-tour-les-dernieres-informations-et-reactions_6245747_823448.html|access-date=2 July 2024|work=Le Monde|date=2 July 2024|archive-date=2 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240702070335/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/02/en-direct-legislatives-2024-suivez-la-campagne-du-second-tour-les-dernieres-informations-et-reactions_6245747_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref> a view also echoed by the leadership of the [[French Communist Party]].<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives : les propos controversés de certains candidats " n'ont pas leur place au sein du RN ", assure Jordan Bardella|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/direct-legislatives-la-campagne-dans-sa-ligne-droite-finale-macron-reunit-le-conseil-des-ministres-03-07-2024-MCEYQOGFJJHSLLPF4QSVVILWUQ.php|access-date=3 July 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=3 July 2024|archive-date=6 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240706000909/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/direct-legislatives-la-campagne-dans-sa-ligne-droite-finale-macron-reunit-le-conseil-des-ministres-03-07-2024-MCEYQOGFJJHSLLPF4QSVVILWUQ.php|url-status=live}}</ref>

The Republicans ultimately chose not to give any voting instructions for the second round.<ref name="LMlive"/>

According to RN deputy [[Sébastien Chenu]], a number of deputies, including those belonging to Ensemble, reached out to ask third-placed RN candidates to withdraw in order to block candidates of the left from winning in the second round, a request which Chenu indicated the party's leadership would consider.<ref name="LMlive2">{{cite news|title=En direct, législatives 2024 : Bruno Le Maire appelle à « voter pour un candidat du camp social-démocrate » dont il exclut La France insoumise|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/01/en-direct-resultats-des-legislatives-suivez-la-campagne-d-entre-deux-tours-et-posez-vos-questions_6245747_823448.html|access-date=1 July 2024|work=Le Monde|date=1 July 2024|archive-date=1 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240701051326/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/01/en-direct-resultats-des-legislatives-suivez-la-campagne-d-entre-deux-tours-et-posez-vos-questions_6245747_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref>

According to the classifications of ''[[Le Monde]]'', 89 three-way and 2 four-way runoffs remained after the publicly announced withdrawals of 134 NFP-supported and 82 Ensemble-supported candidates.<ref name="LMwithdrawals">{{cite news|last1=Breteau|first1=Pierre|last2=Vaudano|first2=Maxime|last3=Derœux|first3=Iris|last4=Parienté|first4=Jonathan|last5=Berhouet|first5=Patxi|last6=Geoffroy|first6=Romain|title=Législatives 2024 : qui sera candidat au second tour après les désistements ? Suivez le décompte en temps réel|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/les-decodeurs/article/2024/07/01/legislatives-2024-qui-sera-candidat-au-second-tour-suivez-le-decompte-en-temps-reel_6245837_4355771.html|access-date=2 July 2024|work=Le Monde|date=1 July 2024|language=fr|archive-date=1 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240701155239/https://www.lemonde.fr/les-decodeurs/article/2024/07/01/legislatives-2024-qui-sera-candidat-au-second-tour-suivez-le-decompte-en-temps-reel_6245837_4355771.html|url-status=live}}</ref> All but 5 NFP candidates withdrew in races where they placed 3rd or below in the first round and RN-backed candidates also qualified, compared to 15 Ensemble candidates (of which 9 were in races where LFI qualified) and 12 [[The Republicans (France)|The Republicans]] or [[miscellaneous right]] candidates (of which 5 were in races where LFI qualified) in the same situation.<ref name="results2024"/><ref name="LMwithdrawals"/> Two candidates who also initially registered for the second round – Dominique Despras in [[Rhône's 8th constituency]] and France Moreau in [[Maine-et-Loire's 5th constituency]] – changed their mind after finding out about other candidates' registrations in the second round. Because they were unable to officially withdraw at this point, they declined to submit any of their paper ballots, meaning that voters did not find paper ballots with the name of either candidate at polling stations.<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives 2024 : triangulaires, désistements, report de voix… À quoi va ressembler le second tour ?|url=https://www.sudouest.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-2024-triangulaires-desistements-report-de-voix-a-quoi-va-ressembler-le-second-tour-20407246.php|access-date=3 July 2024|work=Sud Ouest|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=3 July 2024|archive-date=4 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240704063257/https://www.sudouest.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-2024-triangulaires-desistements-report-de-voix-a-quoi-va-ressembler-le-second-tour-20407246.php|url-status=live}}</ref>

===Second round===
Provisional results placed turnout in the second round at 66.63%, the highest level since [[1997 French legislative election|1997]].<ref>{{Cite tweet|last=Gallard|first=Mathieu|user=mathieugallard|number=1809969496733384841|date=7 July 2024|title=🇫🇷🗳️ L'estimation de la participation finale par les différents instituts : Ifop : 67,5% Harris : 67,1% Elabe : 67,1% OpinionWay : 67% Ipsos : 67% Plus de cohérence qu'au premier tour 🙃|access-date=7 July 2024}}</ref><ref name="results2024"/>

Contrary to pre-election projections, NFP-supported candidates won the largest number of seats after the second round, with Ensemble candidates also beating expectations by coming second ahead of RN-supported candidates in third, trailed by LR candidates in fourth place. According to candidate labeling by the [[Minister of the Interior (France)|Ministry of the Interior]], candidates belonging to NFP parties received 180<!-- PLEASE DO NOT CHANGE, see footnote B: calculated according to the official figures of the Ministry of the Interior, NOT according to the unofficial candidate classifications created by various other media outlets --> seats (well short of the 289 needed for a majority),{{efn|name="NFPtotal"}} compared to 159<!-- PLEASE DO NOT CHANGE, see footnote C: calculated according to the official figures of the Ministry of the Interior, NOT according to the unofficial candidate classifications created by various other media outlets --> for those belonging to Ensemble parties,{{efn|name="Etotal"}} 142 for RN-supported candidates, and 39 for LR candidates, resulting in no party controlling a parliamentary majority. Unofficial media classifications of candidates' affiliations may differ slightly from those used by the Ministry of Interior: according to ''Le Monde'''s analysis, 182 NFP-affiliated candidates were elected, compared with 168 for Ensemble, 143 for the RN, and 45 for LR,<ref name="LMlive6"/><ref name="results2024"/> with 80 constituencies shifting rightwards and 75 shifting leftwards.<ref name="LMlive7"/> The PS more than doubled its number of elected deputies compared to 2022 and the RN gained the second-most seats, while Renaissance suffered the most significant losses of any individual party.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Marchal |first1=Raphaël |last2=Kagni |first2=Maxence |title=Législatives 2024 : Quels équilibres au sein des blocs de la nouvelle Assemblée nationale ? |url=https://lcp.fr/actualites/legislatives-2024-quels-equilibres-au-sein-des-blocs-de-la-nouvelle-assemblee-nationale |access-date=9 July 2024 |work=LCP |date=8 July 2024 |archive-date=9 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240709000846/https://lcp.fr/actualites/legislatives-2024-quels-equilibres-au-sein-des-blocs-de-la-nouvelle-assemblee-nationale |url-status=live }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Wiels |first1=Jason |last2=Marchal |first2=Raphaël |title=Les principales forces politiques en présence à l&#039;Assemblée nationale en chiffres |url=https://lcp.fr/actualites/les-principales-forces-politiques-en-presence-a-l-assemblee-nationale-en-chiffres-122925 |access-date=9 July 2024 |work=LCP |date=20 June 2022 |archive-date=9 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240709084502/https://lcp.fr/actualites/les-principales-forces-politiques-en-presence-a-l-assemblee-nationale-en-chiffres-122925 |url-status=live }}</ref>

An Ipsos survey suggested that the "[[Republican Front (French Fifth Republic)|republican front]]" against the RN remained fairly strong in the second round, with first-round NFP voters supporting Ensemble candidates over RN ones by a 72%–3% margin in second-round duels and first-round Ensemble voters supporting PS/LE/PCF candidates over RN ones by a 54%–15% margin in second-round duels. NFP voters also backed LR candidates over RN ones in second-round duels by a 70%–2% margin, and Ensemble voters by a 79%–4% margin. Even in the case of LFI–RN duels, first-round Ensemble voters supported LFI candidates over RN ones by a 43%–19% margin.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Berrod|first1=Nicolas|title=Législatives 2024 : le « front républicain » a-t-il marché ? Découvrez les reports de voix au second tour|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-2024-le-front-republicain-a-t-il-marche-decouvrez-les-reports-de-voix-au-second-tour-07-07-2024-PH4OJQ4RZZGGDLHABPFRE7ILAE.php|access-date=7 July 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=7 July 2024|archive-date=8 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240708153140/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-2024-le-front-republicain-a-t-il-marche-decouvrez-les-reports-de-voix-au-second-tour-07-07-2024-PH4OJQ4RZZGGDLHABPFRE7ILAE.php|url-status=live}}</ref>

The number of women elected to the National Assembly declined for the second election in a row, from 215 in 2022 to 208 (36%), with the NFP having the highest share at 41% followed by Ensemble with 39%, RN-supported deputies with 32%, and LR with 27%. The average age of the National Assembly remained similar at 49 years and 2 months, with the RN having both the youngest ([[Flavien Termet]], 22) and oldest ([[José Gonzalez (French politician)|José Gonzalez]], 81) deputies. The average age of the RN-supported and NFP deputies was 47, compared to 51 for Ensemble and 52 for LR. Out of the 577 elected deputies, 408 were re-elected, with the highest rate of re-election for Ensemble and LR deputies (both roughly 84.5%) followed by NFP (63%) and RN-supported (57%) deputies. The managerial and professional class is overwhelmingly overrepresented among these 577 deputies, accounting for more than 60% of all new elected officials, with this percentage being similar among all four of the largest groupings. Only three blue-collar workers were elected (0.5% of the National Assembly), compared to their share of 19% in the overall population.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Imbach |first1=Romain |last2=Geoffroy |first2=Romain |title=Age, sexe, profession : qui sont les nouveaux députés ? |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/les-decodeurs/article/2024/07/08/age-sexe-profession-qui-sont-les-nouveaux-deputes_6247938_4355770.html |access-date=9 July 2024 |work=Le Monde |date=8 July 2024 |archive-date=9 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240709114211/https://www.lemonde.fr/les-decodeurs/article/2024/07/08/age-sexe-profession-qui-sont-les-nouveaux-deputes_6247938_4355770.html |url-status=live }}</ref>

For the first time in their history, the RN managed to elect candidates in [[List of constituencies of the National Assembly of France#Overseas: 27 constituencies|overseas constituencies]]:<ref name=":02">{{Cite web|date=7 July 2024|title=Résultats des législatives 2024 à Mayotte et à la Réunion : le RN envoie ses deux premiers députés ultramarins à l'Assemblée nationale|url=https://www.liberation.fr/politique/elections/resultats-des-legislatives-2024-a-mayotte-et-a-la-reunion-le-rn-envoie-ses-deux-premiers-deputes-ultramarins-a-lassemblee-nationale-20240707_D6KOJBXY6FAI7PZMNV25YNVSOI/|access-date=8 July 2024|website=[[Libération]]|language=fr|archive-date=8 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240708003627/https://www.liberation.fr/politique/elections/resultats-des-legislatives-2024-a-mayotte-et-a-la-reunion-le-rn-envoie-ses-deux-premiers-deputes-ultramarins-a-lassemblee-nationale-20240707_D6KOJBXY6FAI7PZMNV25YNVSOI/|url-status=live}}</ref><ref name=":12">{{Cite web|date=8 July 2024|title=Cinque risultati sorprendenti dalle elezioni in Francia|url=https://www.ilpost.it/2024/07/08/elezioni-francesi-vittoria-sinistra/|access-date=8 July 2024|website=[[Il Post]]|language=it|archive-date=10 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240710214744/https://www.ilpost.it/2024/07/08/elezioni-francesi-vittoria-sinistra/|url-status=live}}</ref> [[Anchya Bamana]], contesting in [[Mayotte's 2nd constituency]], and [[Joseph Rivière (politician)|Joseph Rivière]], running in [[Réunion's 3rd constituency]], both won a seat in the National Assembly.<ref name=":02"/> The result in [[Mayotte]] was linked to the [[2024 Mayotte crisis|political crisis affecting the region]] earlier in 2024.<ref name=":12"/>

[[Emmanuel Tjibaou]], the son of late [[Kanak people|Kanak]] independence leader [[Jean-Marie Tjibaou]], was elected to the National Assembly for [[New Caledonia's 2nd constituency]]:<ref name=":1">{{Cite news|date=8 July 2024|title=New Caledonia: historic win for pro-independence candidate in French elections|url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/article/2024/jul/08/france-election-new-caledonia-kanak-emmanuel-tjibaou-seat|access-date=8 July 2024|work=[[The Guardian]]|issn=0261-3077|archive-date=10 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240710214808/https://www.theguardian.com/world/article/2024/jul/08/france-election-new-caledonia-kanak-emmanuel-tjibaou-seat|url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web|last=Decloitre|first=Patrick|date=8 July 2024|title=French election: newcomers in New Caledonia, French Polynesia|url=https://www.rnz.co.nz/international/pacific-news/521542/french-election-newcomers-in-new-caledonia-french-polynesia|access-date=8 July 2024|website=[[RNZ]]|archive-date=7 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240707212642/https://www.rnz.co.nz/international/pacific-news/521542/french-election-newcomers-in-new-caledonia-french-polynesia|url-status=live}}</ref> in the process, he became the first [[Pro-independence movement|pro-independence]] candidate to win a seat since 1986, and his victory was seen as a setback for the French loyalist movement in [[New Caledonia]], in the aftermath of the [[2024 New Caledonia unrest|civil unrest across the archipelago]] earlier in the year.<ref name=":1"/> [[Peio Dufau]] became the first left-wing ''[[abertzale]]'' candidate to get elected to the National Assembly, having run under the banner of [[Euskal Herria Bai]] (EH Bai), supported by the NFP, in [[Pyrénées-Atlantiques's 6th constituency]].<ref>{{cite news|last1=Villepreux|first1=Thomas|title=Législatives au Pays basque : EH Bai a présenté le bon candidat, au bon endroit, au bon moment|url=https://www.sudouest.fr/elections/legislatives/pyrenees-atlantiques/legislatives-au-pays-basque-eh-bai-a-presente-le-bon-candidat-au-bon-endroit-au-bon-moment-20480344.php|access-date=8 July 2024|work=Sud Ouest|date=8 July 2024|archive-date=8 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240708223832/https://www.sudouest.fr/elections/legislatives/pyrenees-atlantiques/legislatives-au-pays-basque-eh-bai-a-presente-le-bon-candidat-au-bon-endroit-au-bon-moment-20480344.php|url-status=live}}</ref>
