==Aftermath==
{{see also|2024-2025 French political crisis}}
In his year-end address on 31 December 2024, Macron acknowledged that calling the election had "brought more division in the (National) Assembly than solutions for the French" and added that "I take my full part for that".<ref>{{cite news|last1=Leicester |first1=John |title=France’s Macron acknowledges that dissolving parliament in 2024 backfired but celebrates Olympics |url=https://apnews.com/article/france-macron-olympics-notre-dame-new-year-elections-33f053c0b06db550d177bb89357a0ba5 |access-date=1 January 2025 |work=AP News |date=1 January 2025}}</ref>
 
===Potential outcomes===
[[File:Place de la République, Juillet 7 2024 06.jpg|thumb|Celebrations on the [[Place de la République]] in Paris on 7 July]]
Although the [[president of France]] theoretically has the power to appoint any individual as [[Prime Minister of France|prime minister]], the likelihood of a [[motion of no confidence]] means that in practice, tradition dictates that the president must nominate someone from any political bloc with an [[absolute majority]] of seats in the incoming [[National Assembly (France)|National Assembly]], resulting in [[Cohabitation (government)#France|cohabitation]] in the event of an opposition victory. When no political force obtains an absolute majority of seats, any government will face the constant threat of a motion of no confidence and handle legislation on a case-by-case basis unless a coalition is secured to avoid this threat.<ref name="LEMazuir"/>

Due to the tripolarisation of the electorate, unprecedented institutional deadlock is a significant possibility if no bloc proves able to secure a majority of votes in the National Assembly to insulate themselves from a motion of no confidence. [[Snap election]]s can only be called at least a year after the previous legislative election under the [[Constitution of France|constitution]].<ref name="LEMazuir">{{cite news|last1=Mazuir|first1=Valérie|title=Législatives 2024 : les scénarios de l'après-7 juillet|url=https://www.lesechos.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-2024-les-scenarios-de-lapres-7-juillet-2102694|access-date=30 June 2024|work=Les Echos|date=20 June 2024|archive-date=29 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240629090814/https://www.lesechos.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-2024-les-scenarios-de-lapres-7-juillet-2102694|url-status=live}}</ref> Some analysts also envisaged the possibility of an [[Technocratic government (Italy)|Italian-style technocratic government]] or a [[2019–2020 Belgian government formation#Formateur Sophie Wilmès (16 March 2020 – 17 March 2020)|2020 Belgian-like temporary minority government]] of independent figures prior to a second snap election.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Dupont|first1=Laureline|title=Quel gouvernement après le 7 juillet ? Les trois scénarios secrets sur la table de Macron|url=https://www.lexpress.fr/politique/quel-gouvernement-apres-le-7-juillet-les-trois-scenarios-secrets-sur-la-table-de-macron-ZXM23QT27VDTDLQSS7KNRT6MZM/|access-date=30 June 2024|work=L'Express|date=26 June 2024|archive-date=29 June 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240629155141/https://www.lexpress.fr/politique/quel-gouvernement-apres-le-7-juillet-les-trois-scenarios-secrets-sur-la-table-de-macron-ZXM23QT27VDTDLQSS7KNRT6MZM/|url-status=live}}</ref>

===Post-election manoeuvring===
Attal announced that he would resign as prime minister just after the results were announced. Macron was not required to accept Attal's resignation, and the latter noted that he would be willing to remain in his post as long as necessary,<ref>{{cite news|last1=Guez|first1=Ariel|title=Législatives: Emmanuel Macron peut-il refuser la démission de Gabriel Attal après l'annonce des résultats?|url=https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/legislatives-emmanuel-macron-peut-il-refuser-la-demission-de-gabriel-attal-apres-l-annonce-des-resultats_AV-202407070580.html|access-date=8 July 2024|work=BFMTV|date=7 July 2024|archive-date=10 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240710214750/https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/elections/legislatives/legislatives-emmanuel-macron-peut-il-refuser-la-demission-de-gabriel-attal-apres-l-annonce-des-resultats_AV-202407070580.html|url-status=live}}</ref> and Macron ultimately refused his resignation "for the time being" on the morning of 8 July.<ref name="LMlive7"/> In a letter published in the regional press on 10 July, Macron declared that "nobody won" the elections and added that the current government would remain in place until it was clear that a new "necessarily plural" government of "political forces that recognise themselves in republican institutions" could be formed,<ref name="LMlive9"/> with leading figures on the left decrying the letter as a "refus[al] to recognise the result of the elections" showing that Macron was "in denial" and attempting a "democratic coup" by signaling that he would not allow the NFP to lead the next government if it included LFI members.<ref>{{cite news |title=DIRECT. Lettre aux Français : Emmanuel Macron "refuse de reconnaître le résultat des urnes", juge Jean-Luc Mélenchon |url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/direct-legislatives-les-deputes-rn-et-modem-font-leur-entree-a-lassemblee-ce-mercredi-10-07-2024-ZEV6NCDEFZFEHAQU2B52B4KU4Y.php |access-date=10 July 2024 |work=Le Parisien |date=10 July 2024 |archive-date=13 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240713031503/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/direct-legislatives-les-deputes-rn-et-modem-font-leur-entree-a-lassemblee-ce-mercredi-10-07-2024-ZEV6NCDEFZFEHAQU2B52B4KU4Y.php |url-status=live }}</ref> Macron accepted his resignation on 16 July,<ref name="LPlive"/> allowing ministers to vote for the president of the National Assembly while remaining in place as a caretaker government.<ref name="LMlive14"/>

In an interview on 1 July, [[Aurore Bergé]] signaled openness to a coalition with members of other parties, including "the Republicans who didn't want to corrupt themselves with Éric Ciotti and with the RN, with certain members of the Socialist Party, the ecologists, the communists,"<ref name="LMlive2"/> a view shared by the leader of alliance partner [[Horizons (political party)|Horizons]] [[Édouard Philippe]].<ref name="LFlive"/> Philippe called for an "agreement which will stabilise the political situation" excluding LFI and the RN. Séjourné likewise excluded the possibility of governing alongside Mélenchon and some of his allies on the left, saying that there would be certain prerequisites for any potential coalition.<ref name="LMlive6">{{cite news|title=En direct, résultats des législatives 2024 : aucune prise de parole d'Emmanuel Macron attendue ce soir « à ce stade », selon l'Elysée|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/07/en-direct-legislatives-2024-on-sait-que-ca-va-impacter-nos-vies_6247441_823448.html|access-date=7 July 2024|work=Le Monde|date=7 July 2024|archive-date=10 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240710214747/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/10/en-direct-assemblee-nationale-melenchon-estime-que-macron-doit-s-incliner-face-au-nfp-le-pen-denonce-un-cirque-indigne-apres-la-lettre-du-president_6247441_823448.html|url-status=live}}</ref> Interviewed on 8 July, Darmanin envisaged the possibility of cooperation with the PS on some issues where they differed from LFI,<ref name="LMlive7"/> but went on to add that he was opposed to working with ecologist deputies.<ref name="LMlive9"/> On 9 July, several Renaissance deputies threatened to file a motion of no confidence in the event that the next government included LFI deputies, and in the face of these threats and Attal's continuation as prime minister, the NFP warned Macron "against any attempt to hijack the institutions."<ref name="LMlive8"/>

A number of key figures indicated their preference for working with the right rather than the left, with Philippe arguing for a "technical agreement" but not coalition with LR in addition to Darmanin publicly stating that "the country is on the right[, so] we must govern on the right," and Macron reportedly met with LR Senate president [[Gérard Larcher]] on the evening of 8 July.<ref name="LMlive8"/><ref>{{cite news |last1=Jacquot |first1=Guillaume |title=Législatives : les macronistes entament de longues tractations pour tenter de faire émerger une coalition centrale |url=https://www.publicsenat.fr/actualites/politique/legislatives-les-macronistes-entament-de-longues-tractations-pour-tenter-de-faire-emerger-une-coalition-centrale |access-date=9 July 2024 |work=Public Sénat |date=8 July 2024 |archive-date=9 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240709105733/https://www.publicsenat.fr/actualites/politique/legislatives-les-macronistes-entament-de-longues-tractations-pour-tenter-de-faire-emerger-une-coalition-centrale |url-status=live }}</ref> Bergé and Darmanin both publicly appealed for the support of LR deputies the following day, with the latter also confirming that he would also vote for a motion of no confidence against a NFP government, but Bayrou was less receptive to the idea, suggesting that he preferred a coalition which still involved some figures from the left.<ref name="LMlive9">{{cite news |title=En direct, Assemblée nationale : Emmanuel Macron conditionne la nomination d'un premier ministre à la création d'une majorité " nécessairement plurielle " à l'Assemblée nationale |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/10/en-direct-legislatives-2024-les-deputes-renaissance-favorables-a-une-coalition-de-projet-allant-des-sociaux-democrates-a-la-droite-de-gouvernement_6247441_823448.html |access-date=10 July 2024 |work=Le Monde |date=10 July 2024 |archive-date=10 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240710214747/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/10/en-direct-assemblee-nationale-melenchon-estime-que-macron-doit-s-incliner-face-au-nfp-le-pen-denonce-un-cirque-indigne-apres-la-lettre-du-president_6247441_823448.html |url-status=live }}</ref>

On 2 July, LFI national coordinator [[Manuel Bompard]] announced that his party would not participate in a [[grand coalition]] including LFI and Ensemble,<ref name="LFlive">{{cite news|title=EN DIRECT – Élections législatives 2024 : «Le gouvernement est prêt», assure Marine Le Pen, qui confirme qu'elle n'en fera pas partie|url=https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/en-direct-elections-legislatives-2024-circonscriptions-sondages-second-tour-20240702|access-date=2 July 2024|work=Le Figaro|issue=2 July 2024|archive-date=2 July and Attal likewise ruled out the possibility of a coalition with LFI.<ref name="LMlive3"/> Tondelier declined to rule out the possibility of participating in a coalition but indicated her desire not to do so and her opposition to a Macron-aligned prime minister.<ref>{{cite news|title=EN DIRECT – Élections législatives 2024 : «On a perdu un trimestre de croissance» à cause de l'instabilité politique, lance le patron des petites et moyennes entreprises|url=https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/en-direct-elections-legislatives-2024-resultats-sondages-7-juillet-circonscriptions-candidats-20240703|access-date=3 July 2024|work=Le "confiant"|url=https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/en-direct-legislatives-2024-sondages-resultats-deuxieme-tour-candidat-20240705|access-date=5 July 2024|work=Le Figaro|date=5 July 2024|archive-date=5 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240705072719/https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/en-direct-legislatives-2024-sondages-resultats-deuxieme-tour-candidat-20240705|url-status=live}}</ref> Just after the second round, Mélenchon called for the appointment of a prime minister from the left, echoed by Tondelier and Faure, who said that the NFP intended to govern and would not support any Ensemble-led coalition.<ref name="LMlive6"/> [[Yannick Jadot]] announced that the NFP would propose its government the week of the second round, Faure declared that the alliance would agree upon a name for prime minister by then, Bompard said that the NFP would implement its programme in its entirety,<ref name="LMlive7">{{cite news|title=En direct, législatives 2024 : les dirigeants du Nouveau Front populaire veulent présenter « une candidature » au poste de premier ministre « dans la semaine »|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/08/en-direct-legislatives-2024-gabriel-attal-doit-presenter-lundi-sa-demission-a-emmanuel-macron_6247441_823448.html|access-date=8 July 2024|work=Le Monde|date=8 July 2024|archive-date=8 July and [[Sandrine Rousseau]] pledged not to repeatedly invoke [[article 49 of the French Constitution#Commitment of responsibility on a bill (49.3)|article 49.3]] unlike recent governments.<ref>{{cite news|title=DIRECT. Législatives : " Nous laissons l'Assemblée nationale se constituer ", indique l'entourage de Macron|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-le-nouveau-front-populaire-majoritaire-a-lassemblee-attal-presente-sa-demission-suivez-notre-direct-au-lendemain-du-second-tour-ce-matin-08-07-2024-22ARSNVTXRAP5GUTYJLKN3HU7I.php|access-date=8 July 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=8 July 2024|archive-date=8 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240708153711/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-le-nouveau-front-populaire-majoritaire-a-lassemblee-attal-presente-sa-demission-suivez-notre-direct-au-lendemain-du-second-tour-ce-matin-08-07-2024-22ARSNVTXRAP5GUTYJLKN3HU7I.php|url-status=live}}</ref>

PS alliance negotiator [[Johanna Rolland]], along with [[Carole Delga]], welcomed the potential support of the leftmost Ensemble deputies in a NFP-led coalition,<ref>{{cite news |title=DIRECT. Législatives : les députés insoumis font leur rentrée des classes à l'Assemblée nationale |url-status=live }}</ref><ref name="LMlive9"/> while Faure resisted pressure from Macron allies to break away from LFI in order to form a government.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Cassini |first1=Sandrine |title=Le Nouveau Front populaire sous pression pour se mettre d'accord sur un premier ministre |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/07/11/au-nouveau-front-populaire-une-course-contre-la-montre-pour-s-accorder-sur-un-premier-ministre_6248509_823448.html |access-date=11 July 2024 |work=Le Monde |date=11 July 2024 |archive-date=11 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240711061647/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/07/11/au-nouveau-front-populaire-une-course-contre-la-montre-pour-s-accorder-sur-un-premier-ministre_6248509_823448.html |url-status=live }}</ref> [[Huguette Bello]] emerged as a possible name for prime minister on 12 July, proposed by Roussel but resisted by the PS, which failed to approve Bello's candidacy on 13 July and called for further discussions.<ref name="LMlive12"/> LFI reacted by suspending negotiations, demanding that all parties agree upon on a single candidacy for the presidency of the National Assembly, and refusing the possibility of a civil society figure being appointed prime minister, after which the PS, LE, and PCF pushed for discussions to resume and proposed appointing a civil society figure as prime minister,<ref name="LMlive13"/> [[Laurence Tubiana]],<ref>{{cite news |title=Le PS, les écologistes et les communistes devraient proposer aux insoumis le nom de Laurence Tubiana pour occuper le poste de Premier ministre |url=https://www.francetvinfo.fr/elections/direct-legislatives-2024-le-nouveau-front-populaire-sous-pression-pour-s-accorder-sur-un-nom-de-premier-ministre_6667281.html |access-date=15 July 2024 |work=franceinfo |date=15 July 2024}}</ref> a hypothesis publicly rejected by LFI figureheads as too "Macron-compatible."<ref name="LPlive">{{cite news |title=DIRECT. Législatives : Gérald Darmanin appelle le camp présidentiel à "travailler avec LR" |url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/direct-legislatives-un-conseil-des-ministres-a-11h30-laurence-tubiana-proposee-pour-matignon-par-le-ps-et-le-pc-16-07-2024-NGAFO5QLHBCGNLRZJTTFXWXHLU.php |access-date=16 July 2024 |work=Le Parisien |date=16 July 2024}}</ref> Tubiana dismissed the possibility of becoming prime minister on 22 July.<ref>{{cite news |title=Laurence Tubiana renonce à être candidate au poste de premier ministre car son nom " a rencontré des oppositions au sein du NFP " |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/07/22/laurence-tubiana-renonce-a-se-porter-candidate-au-poste-de-premier-ministre_6255311_823448.html |access-date=22 July 2024 |work=Le Monde |agency=Agence France-Presse |date=22 July 2024}}</ref> On 23 July, the NFP announced that it would propose 37-year-old civil servant [[Lucie Castets]], director of finance and purchasing for the city of Paris, for the post of prime minister, though Macron will not appoint a new government until mid-August at earliest and noted that the question was not of the name for prime minister but rather the ability to find a majority to govern.<ref name="LMlive15">{{cite news |title=En direct : Lucie Castets proposée par le Nouveau Front populaire comme candidate au poste de première ministre |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/23/en-direct-lucie-castets-proposee-par-le-nouveau-front-populaire-comme-candidate-au-poste-de-premiere-ministre_6256433_823448.html |access-date=23 July 2024 |work=Le Monde |date=23 July 2024}}</ref>

[[Laurent Wauquiez]] ruled out the possibility of LR participating in a potential coalition just after the results were announced.<ref name="LMlive6"/> President of the [[Senate Republicans|LR group in the Senate]] [[Bruno Retailleau]] ruled out the possibility of working with any coalition of the left, and like others within his party, deemed the LR brand to be "dead."<ref name="LMlive7"/> Despite these statements, some LR figures still called for a pro-Macron alliance in the National Assembly, including [[Xavier Bertrand]] and [[Olivier Marleix]].<ref name="LMlive8"/> After being elected president of the group, Wauquiez proclaimed that he would not agree to a coalition but would be open to a "legislative pact," and also signaled that the right would vote for a [[motion of no confidence]] if any future government included LFI members,<ref name="LMlive9"/> a position also held by Larcher.<ref name="LMlive10">{{cite news |title=En direct, la situation politique en France : pour François Bayrou, l'impulsion ne viendra pas des partis mais d'Emmanuel Macron qui " devra nommer un premier ministre " rassembleur |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/11/en-direct-la-situation-politique-en-france-les-dernieres-informations-et-reaction-apres-la-nouvelle-lettre-d-emmanuel-macron_6247441_823448.html |access-date=11 July 2024 |work=Le Monde |date=11 July 2024 |archive-date=11 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240711055041/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/11/en-direct-la-situation-politique-en-france-les-dernieres-informations-et-reaction-apres-la-nouvelle-lettre-d-emmanuel-macron_6247441_823448.html |url-status=live }}</ref>

After falling short of pre-election expectations, Le Pen said that the RN's victory "is only postponed" and that she could not be disappointed with the party's gains in the election.<ref name="LMlive6"/> On 8 July, [[Sébastien Chenu]] appeared to express regret about the controversies surrounding many of the candidates who went on to lose their races, and affirmed that the RN would remain in opposition "without compromise,"<ref name="LMlive7"/> and [[Zoltán Kovács (politician, born 1969)|Zoltán Kovács]] announced that Bardella would chair the [[Patriots for Europe]] group in the [[European Parliament]].<ref>{{cite news|title=Parlement européen : Jordan Bardella va présider un nouveau groupe nationaliste initié par le Premier ministre hongrois, Viktor Orban|url=https://www.francetvinfo.fr/politique/jordan-bardella/parlement-europeen-jordan-bardella-va-presider-un-nouveau-groupe-nationaliste-initie-par-le-premier-ministre-hongrois-viktor-orban_6654060.html|access-date=8 July 2024|work=franceinfo|agency=Agence France-Presse|date=8 July 2024|archive-date=8 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240708222005/https://www.francetvinfo.fr/politique/jordan-bardella/parlement-europeen-jordan-bardella-va-presider-un-nouveau-groupe-nationaliste-initie-par-le-premier-ministre-hongrois-viktor-orban_6654060.html|url-status=live}}</ref> Gilles Pennelle, the general director of the party who oversaw the selection of RN candidates, resigned the day after the election.<ref name="LMlive7"/> On 11 July, [[Renaud Labaye]] initially announced that the RN would not automatically vote for a motion of no confidence in a NFP-led government including LFI members, but rather consider legislative texts on a case-by-case basis,<ref>{{cite news |last1=Bordas |first1=Wally |last2=Gentilhomme |first2=Célestine |title=Législatives : le RN ne censurerait pas automatiquement un gouvernement NFP avec des ministres Insoumis |url=https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-le-rn-ne-censurerait-pas-automatiquement-un-gouvernement-nfp-avec-des-ministres-insoumis-20240711 |access-date=11 July 2024 |work=Le Figaro |date=11 July 2024 |archive-date=12 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240712025031/https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-le-rn-ne-censurerait-pas-automatiquement-un-gouvernement-nfp-avec-des-ministres-insoumis-20240711 |url-status=live }}</ref> but Le Pen subsequently clarified that the RN would do so in the case that any government contained LFI or LE ministers, regardless of who led it,<ref name="LMlive10"/> and Bardella confirmed that they would immediately vote for a motion of no confidence in any NFP minority government.<ref>{{cite news |title=DIRECT. Législatives : le RN censurera "tout gouvernement" avec des ministres insoumis ou écologistes, annonce Marine Le Pen |url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/direct-legislatives-macron-estime-que-personne-na-emporte-les-elections-les-oppositions-sinsurgent-11-07-2024-5QOUO66FEJECDEGOYQ7OXTPQWE.php |access-date=11 July 2024 |work=Le Parisien |date=11 July 2024 |archive-date=11 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240711082004/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/direct-legislatives-macron-estime-que-personne-na-emporte-les-elections-les-oppositions-sinsurgent-11-07-2024-5QOUO66FEJECDEGOYQ7OXTPQWE.php |url-status=live }}</ref>

===Prime Ministerial appointment===
====Appointment background====
After the dissolution of the [[16th legislature of the French Fifth Republic|16th legislature]] by Macron on 9 June 2024, the [[2024 French legislative elections|early legislative elections]] took place on 30 June and 7 July. While the [[National Rally]] was originally anticipated to obtain a relative majority, it came third behind the [[New Popular Front]] and [[Ensemble (political coalition)|Ensemble]].

Then-Prime Minister [[Gabriel Attal]], having only served six months in office, presented his resignation to  Macron, who accepted it on 16 July. The day before the opening of the [[2024 Summer Olympic Games|Paris Olympic Games]], the New Popular Front proposed that [[Lucie Castets]] be nominated as prime minister. In reaction, arguing that "no one won [the elections]",  Macron announced the holding of consultations to form a government.<ref>{{Cite news|title=Résultats législatives 2024 : Emmanuel Macron lance les grandes manœuvres (et assure que « personne n'a gagné ») |url=https://www.20minutes.fr/politique/4100751-20240710-resultats-legislatives-2024-emmanuel-macron-lance-grandes-man-uvres-assure-personne-gagne |work=20 Minutes |date=10 July 2024 |access-date=5 September 2024 |language=fr}}</ref>

On 16 August, at the end of the Olympic Games, Macron invited party leaders and presidents of parliamentary groups from both chambers to the [[Palais de l'Élysée]] on 23 August to try to form a government.<ref>{{Cite news|title=Emmanuel Macron convie les chefs de partis le 23 août, pas de Premier ministre dans l'immédiat |url=https://www.lavoixdunord.fr/1492981/article/2024-08-16/emmanuel-macron-convie-les-chefs-de-partie-le-23-aout-pas-de-premier-ministre |work=La Voix du Nord |date=16 August 2024 |access-date=5 September 2024 |language=fr}}</ref> After the President received the party leaders and the presidents of parliamentary groups, Macron's office announced in a press release on 26 August that Castets would not be appointed prime minister.<ref>{{Cite news|title=Nouveau gouvernement : Emmanuel Macron refuse de nommer Lucie Castets et lance de nouvelles consultations|url=https://www.lesechos.fr/politique-societe/emmanuel-macron-president/nouveau-gouvernement-emmanuel-macron-refuse-de-nommer-lucie-castets-et-lance-de-nouvelles-consultations-2115247 |work=Les Echos |date=26 August 2024 |access-date=5 September 2024 |language=fr}}</ref>

On 2 September, Emmanuel Macron received nominations from [[Bernard Cazeneuve]], the former [[Socialist Party (France)|Socialist Party]] Prime Minister from 2016 to 2017, and [[Xavier Bertrand]], a former [[Hauts-de-France]] region president.<ref>{{Cite news|language=fr |title=Matignon: Macron "test" Cazeneuve and Bertrand, the Beaudet surprise emerges|url=https://information.tv5monde.com/international/matignon-macron-teste-cazeneuve-et-bertrand-la-surprise-beaudet-emerge-2738073 |work=TV5 Monde |date=2 September 2024 |access-date=5 September 2024}}.</ref> Faced with the risk of a motion of censure, the candidacy of [[Michel Barnier]] was considered on 4 September.<ref>{{Cite news|author=|title=Nouveau Premier ministre: Michel Barnier, nouvelle "piste sérieuse" d'Emmanuel Macron?|date=4 September 2024 |url=https://www.bfmtv.com/politique/gouvernement/nouveau-premier-ministre-michel-barnier-nouvelle-piste-serieuse-d-emmanuel-macron_AV-202409040913.htm |work=BFMTV |access-date=5 September 2024 |language=fr}}</ref>

====Final appointment====
{{main|Barnier government}}
On 5 September 2024, [[Michel Barnier]] was appointed as prime minister by Macron, heading a Parliament divided nearly evenly between the leftist New Popular Front, which holds the plurality of seats, Macron's centrist to centre-right Ensemble, and the far-right National Rally.<ref>{{Cite news|date=5 September 2024|title=Live blog: Macron names Michel Barnier new prime minister|language=en-GB|work=France24|url=https://www.france24.com/en/europe/20240905-%F0%9F%94%B4-live-blog-macron-names-michel-barnier-new-prime-minister|access-date=5 September 2024}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |date=5 September 2024 |title=Macron’s Choice of French Premier Shows His Ambitions Unraveling |url=https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2024-09-05/who-is-michel-barnier-france-s-new-prime-minister-and-why-macron-chose-him |access-date=5 September 2024 |work=Bloomberg.com |language=en}}</ref>

While the NFP has announced it would move a [[motion of no confidence]] against any government not led by them, the [[National Rally]] announces that it will wait for the general policy statement of the new government before deciding whether to support any motions of no confidence or censure.<ref>{{Cite news|title=L'ancien ministre Michel Barnier, figure des Républicains, nommé Premier ministre par Emmanuel Macron |date=5 September 2024|url=https://www.francetvinfo.fr/politique/emmanuel-macron/l-ancien-ministre-michel-barnier-figure-des-republicains-nomme-premier-ministre-par-emmanuel-macron_6764575.html |work=Franceinfo |access-date=5 September 2024 |language=fr}}</ref>

===Composition of the National Assembly===
Plans for governance were likely to only be solidified after the formation of [[parliamentary group]]s in the [[17th legislature of the French Fifth Republic]] clarified the alignment of elected deputies starting on 11 July, which was be followed by the election of the next [[president of the National Assembly of France]] on 18 July as well as the appointment of vice presidents, quaestors, and secretaries as part of the {{ill|bureau of the National Assembly of France|fr|Bureau de l'Assemblée nationale française}}.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Beaumont|first1=Olivier|title=Qui pour gouverner ? Le grand flou à l'issue du second tour des législatives|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/qui-pour-gouverner-le-grand-flou-a-lissue-du-second-tour-des-legislatives-08-07-2024-SI4L2HD6SVHCDAXQ5IM5AG6TBY.php|access-date=8 July 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=8 July 2024|archive-date=8 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240708153600/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/qui-pour-gouverner-le-grand-flou-a-lissue-du-second-tour-des-legislatives-08-07-2024-SI4L2HD6SVHCDAXQ5IM5AG6TBY.php|url-status=live}}</ref> Macron is expected to allow the bloc which is able to elect the next president of the National Assembly to form the next government.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Gallet |first1=Ludwig |last2=Beaumont |first2=Olivier |title=Coalition, nouveau gouvernement… Sous pression, Emmanuel Macron temporise |url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/coalition-nouveau-gouvernement-sous-pression-emmanuel-macron-temporise-09-07-2024-BXZT5YTDLJA6XMQ67QD4FRBKL4.php |access-date=10 July 2024 |work=Le Parisien |date=10 July 2024 |archive-date=10 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240710185740/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/coalition-nouveau-gouvernement-sous-pression-emmanuel-macron-temporise-09-07-2024-BXZT5YTDLJA6XMQ67QD4FRBKL4.php |url-status=live }}</ref> Numerous figures on the left also called upon deputies to block the RN from obtaining key posts in the National Assembly,<ref name="LMlive9"/> with pro-Macron deputies potentially also willing to do so.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Bordas |first1=Wally |title=À l'Assemblée, le camp Macron tenté de s'allier avec la gauche pour priver le RN de certains postes clés |url=https://www.lefigaro.fr/elections/legislatives/a-l-assemblee-le-camp-macron-tente-de-s-allier-avec-la-gauche-pour-priver-le-rn-de-certains-poste-cles-20240709 |access-date=10 July 2024 |work=Le Figaro |date=10 July 2024}}</ref> Renaissance deputy [[Yaël Braun-Pivet]] was re-elected president of the National Assembly with 220 votes in the third round of voting on 18 July owing to the support of LR deputies, ahead of NFP-supported PCF deputy [[André Chassaigne]] with 207.<ref name="LMlive14">{{cite news |title=En direct, présidence de l'Assemblée nationale : Yaël Braun-Pivet, candidate à sa succession, en tête au deuxième tour |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/18/en-direct-assemblee-nationale-qui-va-obtenir-la-presidence-les-deputes-ont-commence-a-voter_6249323_823448.html |access-date=18 July 2024 |work=Le Monde |date=18 July 2024}}</ref> Across 19 and 20 July, the NFP obtained 12 of 22 posts in the bureau of the National Assembly, with the RN shut out of all posts.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Fau |first1=Ludovic |title=Assemblée nationale : la gauche devient majoritaire au Bureau, aucun poste pour le RN |url=https://lcp.fr/actualites/assemblee-nationale-la-gauche-devient-majoritaire-au-bureau-aucun-poste-pour-le-rn |access-date=20 July 2024 |work=LCP |date=20 July 2024}}</ref>

Shortly after the elections, [[Clémentine Autain]], like Ruffin, announced that she would not join the [[La France Insoumise group]] in the incoming legislature, instead hoping to form a new group,<ref name="LMlive7"/> potentially alongside [[Christophe Bex]] and LFI incumbents who managed to win re-election against official LFI candidates including [[Alexis Corbière]], [[Hendrik Davi]], and [[Danielle Simonnet]],<ref>{{cite news|title=Législatives : Autain, Ruffin… ces voix désormais dissidentes qui ne siégeront pas avec La France insoumise|url=https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-autain-ruffin-ces-voix-desormais-dissidentes-qui-ne-siegeront-pas-avec-la-france-insoumise-08-07-2024-VO7D6ZRBHJBH7J6OMBLX33UFEE.php|access-date=8 July 2024|work=Le Parisien|date=8 July 2024|archive-date=8 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240708153610/https://www.leparisien.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-autain-ruffin-ces-voix-desormais-dissidentes-qui-ne-siegeront-pas-avec-la-france-insoumise-08-07-2024-VO7D6ZRBHJBH7J6OMBLX33UFEE.php|url-status=live}}</ref> with the five of them seeking to form a new group with members of the PCF, LE, and [[Génération.s]] and Corbière also expressing his willingness to join a unified NFP group,<ref name="LMlive8"/> and all but Ruffin announcing the creation of the political movement [[L'Après]] on 12 July.<ref name="LMlive11">{{cite news |title=En direct : Fabien Roussel propose Huguette Bello, présidente du conseil régional de La Réunion, à Matignon ; les négociations se poursuivent à gauche |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/12/en-direct-la-situation-politique-en-france-elisabeth-borne-dement-etre-candidate-a-la-presidence-du-groupe-de-deputes-renaissance_6247441_823448.html |access-date=12 July 2024 |work=Le Monde |date=12 July 2024 |archive-date=12 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240712053901/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/12/en-direct-la-situation-politique-en-france-elisabeth-borne-dement-etre-candidate-a-la-presidence-du-groupe-de-deputes-renaissance_6247441_823448.html |url-status=live }}</ref> The five deputies ultimately announced that they would join the [[Ecologist Group|Ecologist group]] on 15 July.<ref name="LMlive13">{{cite news |title=En direct, futur premier ministre : LFI annonce suspendre les discussions dans l'attente d'une candidature unique du NFP pour la présidence de l'Assemblée nationale |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/15/en-direct-assemblee-nationale-les-cinq-dissidents-de-la-france-insoumise-siegeront-avec-les-ecologistes_6249323_823448.html |access-date=15 July 2024 |work=Le Monde |date=15 July 2024}}</ref>

The [[Democratic and Republican Left group]] appeared on course to meet the threshold for 15 deputies in the new National Assembly, with Chassaigne counting 8 PCF deputies, 1 [[Republican and Socialist Left]] (GRS) deputy, and "8 or 9" deputies from [[overseas France]].<ref name="LMlive8"/>

Of the 22 deputies in the [[Liberties, Independents, Overseas and Territories]] (LIOT) group before the snap election was called, 14 were re-elected. Because the group is so close to the threshold of 15 deputies needed, negotiations are likely to make the continuation of the group possible in the new National Assembly.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Stromboni |first1=Alain |title=Législatives 2024 : quel avenir pour le groupe Liot et les députés nationalistes à l'Assemblée nationale ? |url=https://france3-regions.francetvinfo.fr/corse/legislatives-2024-quel-avenir-pour-le-groupe-liot-et-les-deputes-nationalistes-a-l-assemblee-nationale-3001073.html |access-date=9 July 2024 |work=France 3 Corse ViaStella |date=8 July 2024 |archive-date=10 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240710190249/https://france3-regions.francetvinfo.fr/corse/legislatives-2024-quel-avenir-pour-le-groupe-liot-et-les-deputes-nationalistes-a-l-assemblee-nationale-3001073.html |url-status=live }}</ref> However, [[Martine Froger]] and [[David Taupiac]], re-elected with the support of the NFP, declined to comment on the subject, as was the case with [[Paul Molac]], [[Jean-Luc Warsmann]], and [[Estelle Youssouffa]], while [[Yannick Favennec-Bécot]] was noncommittal. [[Michel Castellani]], [[Paul-André Colombani]], [[Charles de Courson]], [[Stéphane Lenormand]], [[Max Mathiasin]], [[Christophe Naegelen]], and [[Olivier Serva]] are all committed to re-forming the group, while [[Valérie Létard]] expressed her desire to assert her "independence" as her predecessor [[Béatrice Descamps]] did in the LIOT group.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Ives |first1=Timothée |title=Législatives 2024 : le groupe Liot survivra-t-il à l'Assemblée ? |url=https://www.humanite.fr/politique/assemblee-nationale/legislatives-2024-le-groupe-liot-survivra-t-il-a-lassemblee |access-date=9 July 2024 |work=L'Humanité |date=8 July 2024 |archive-date=11 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240711024226/https://www.humanite.fr/politique/assemblee-nationale/legislatives-2024-le-groupe-liot-survivra-t-il-a-lassemblee |url-status=live }}</ref> Lenormand was elected president of the group of exactly 15 deputies on 16 July.<ref name="LPlive"/>

The Elysée stated that Macron would wait for the new National Assembly to organise itself before making "the necessary decisions."<ref name="LMlive7"/> On 12 July, Attal announced that he would be a candidate for the presidency of the [[Renaissance group]] and that it would be renamed to the "Together for the Republic group" (''groupe Ensemble pour la République'') as well,<ref>{{cite news |title=En direct : Gabriel Attal officialise sa candidature à la présidence du groupe Renaissance à l'Assemblée nationale |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/12/en-direct-la-situation-politique-en-france-elisabeth-borne-dement-etre-candidate-a-la-presidence-du-groupe-de-deputes-renaissance_6247441_823448.html |access-date=12 July 2024 |work=Le Monde |date=12 July 2024 |archive-date=12 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240712053901/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/12/en-direct-la-situation-politique-en-france-elisabeth-borne-dement-etre-candidate-a-la-presidence-du-groupe-de-deputes-renaissance_6247441_823448.html |url-status=live }}</ref> and was elected on 13 July.<ref name="LMlive12"/>

Renaissance deputy [[Sacha Houlié]], representing the left flank of his party, pleaded with his colleagues to form a new "social democratic" group in the National Assembly,<ref>{{cite news|last1=Marie-Leconte|first1=Julie|title=Législatives 2024 : Sacha Houlié réfléchit à constituer un nouveau groupe "social-démocrate" à l'Assemblée nationale|url=https://www.francetvinfo.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-2024-sacha-houlie-reflechit-a-constituer-un-nouveau-groupe-social-democrate-a-l-assemblee-nationale_6653967.html|access-date=8 July 2024|work=franceinfo|date=8 July 2024|archive-date=11 July 2024|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240711024233/https://www.francetvinfo.fr/elections/legislatives/legislatives-2024-sacha-houlie-reflechit-a-constituer-un-nouveau-groupe-social-democrate-a-l-assemblee-nationale_6653967.html|url-status=live}}</ref> and was able to quickly gather 20 deputies for his initiative. With many elected deputies embittered with Macron, only 33 deputies committed to joining the [[Renaissance group]], with others preferring to maintain their leverage and threatening to leave for Houlié's group or join the MoDem in the event of an alliance with the right,<ref name="Renaissancegroup">{{cite news |last1=D’Angelo |first1=Robin |last2=Darame |first2=Mariama |title=Le groupe Renaissance à l'Assemblée nationale au bord de la dislocation |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/07/10/le-groupe-renaissance-a-l-assemblee-nationale-au-bord-de-la-dislocation_6248297_823448.html |access-date=10 July 2024 |work=Le Monde |date=10 July 2024 |archive-date=11 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240711024229/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/article/2024/07/10/le-groupe-renaissance-a-l-assemblee-nationale-au-bord-de-la-dislocation_6248297_823448.html |url-status=live }}</ref> and Houlié officially announced on 10 July that he would not join the Renaissance group, which 40 deputies elected under the banner of Renaissance had yet to join, and instead form his own "ranging from the social right to the socialist left," saying that he didn't "agree with [the pro-Macron line] anymore," adding that he felt closest to the views of Glucksmann.<ref name="LMlive9"/> His efforts were ultimately unsuccessful, with 97 of 98 Renaissance deputies joining the group.<ref name="LMlive12">{{cite news |title=En direct, après les législatives : accusée de " pactiser avec le RN " pour garder la présidence de l'Assemblée, Yaël Braun-Pivet dénonce une polémique " nauséabonde " |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/13/en-direct-gabriel-attal-elu-a-la-tete-du-groupe-renaissance-promet-de-chercher-a-construire-des-ponts-avec-les-forces-politiques-attachees-a-la-republique_6249323_823448.html |access-date=13 July 2024 |work=Le Monde |date=13 July 2024}}</ref>

The [[Horizons group (National Assembly)|Horizons group]] will be re-constituted in the new National Assembly,<ref name="Renaissancegroup"/> as will the [[Democratic, MoDem and Independents group|MoDem group]] to be headed by [[Marc Fesneau]] after being elected president on 10 July against [[Nicolas Turquois]] and previous group president [[Jean-Paul Mattei]], having already led the group between June 2017 and November 2018. However, as a minister in the current government, he must choose to resign from either the government or as deputy.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Hermans |first1=Thomas |title=Marc Fesneau élu patron des députés MoDem à l'Assemblée nationale, tout en restant ministre de l'Agriculture |url=https://france3-regions.francetvinfo.fr/centre-val-de-loire/loir-cher/blois/marc-fesneau-elu-patron-des-deputes-modem-a-l-assemblee-nationale-tout-en-restant-ministre-de-l-agriculture-3002783.html |access-date=10 July 2024 |work=France 3 Centre-Val de Loire |date=10 July 2024 |archive-date=10 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240710190356/https://france3-regions.francetvinfo.fr/centre-val-de-loire/loir-cher/blois/marc-fesneau-elu-patron-des-deputes-modem-a-l-assemblee-nationale-tout-en-restant-ministre-de-l-agriculture-3002783.html |url-status=live }}</ref>

On 9 July, [[Aurélien Pradié]] stated that he believed there would no longer be a [[The Republicans group (National Assembly)|LR group]] within the National Assembly, expecting a change in both their name and way of operation.<ref name="LMlive8">{{cite news |title=En direct, législatives 2024 : Xavier Bertrand et Olivier Marleix veulent un premier ministre issu de LR ; Edouard Philippe plaide pour un « bloc » allant de la droite au camp présidentiel |url=https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/09/en-direct-legislatives-2024-le-nouveau-front-populaire-se-dit-pret-a-gouvernement-des-demain_6247441_823448.html |access-date=9 July 2024 |work=Le Monde |date=9 July 2024 |archive-date=9 July 2024 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20240709173550/https://www.lemonde.fr/politique/live/2024/07/09/en-direct-legislatives-2024-le-nouveau-front-populaire-se-dit-pret-a-gouvernement-des-demain_6247441_823448.html |url-status=live }}</ref> On 10 July, Wauquiez, elected as leader of the group upon his return to the National Assembly, announced that the group would change its name to become "The Republican Right" (''La Droite Républicaine'').<ref name="LMlive9"/>

[[Éric Ciotti]] announced the creation of a new group in the National Assembly called [[On the Right! group|On the Right!]] (''À droite !''), with 15 of 17 LR deputies elected with the support of the RN appearing in a photo posted on social media.<ref name="LMlive8"/>

Bardella also implied that deputies elected with the support of the RN who were implicated in various controversies during the campaign would not sit with the [[National Rally group (National Assembly)|National Rally group]] in the legislature.<ref name="LMlive7"/>
